nityamahimatvAdiliN^gajAtaM, patyAdishabdasamUhashcha chaturmukhe.anavakAsha ityarthaH | anavakAsha iti prAbalyakathanam.h | ityanena prakAreNa, tat.h prAgukttanyAyajAtaM, samastamatra natu kiJNchidevetyarthaH | sarvametatsUchitaM sUtre, "shabdebhyaH' iti Adyatharkabahuvachanena | (ete sarve.api nyAyAH sUtreNaiva vachanavR^ittyupalakShaNAbhyAM darshitAH | ata eva sudhAyAM, "dR^ishyante tAshcha sarvashaH' ityanuvyAkhyAnaM, "sUtrasUchitAnnyAyAnabhidhAya' iti vyAkhyAtam.h | evamuttaratrApi "svayaM bhagavatoditAH' ityAdau draShyavyam.h ) || 14 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNabhAvabodhe prathamAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH ||
anyatraiva prasiddhAvyakttAdishabdasamanvayArthaM chaturthaH pAdaH pravR^ittaH | etatpAdIyAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAH saN^graheNa anuvyAkhyAyAmukttAH sarvamAnavirodhashcha vyutpatterapyashakyatA | parasparavirodhashcha virodhaH kAryatadvatoH | strIliN^gatvaM niShedhashcha yukttayaH pUrvapakShagAH | doShAtyaspR^iShyiniyamaH shabdArthAnekatA tathA | bahurUpatvamIshasya vyakttAvyakttivisheShitA || utpAdanaM svadehAchcha durjanAvyakttAtA tathA | ityAdyA yukttayaH sAkShAtsiddhAntasthApakA iha' iti | OMAnumAnikamapyekeShAmiti chenna, sharIrarUpakavinyastagR^ihIterdarshayati cha OM ityatra, "avyakttAtpuruShaH paraH' iti vAkyagatAvyakttAdishabdavAchyaM kiM pradhAnAdi, uta viShNuriti avaratvAdiliN^gApAditAnyatraprasiddhisamanvayasUtrAbhyAM sandehe, pradhAnAdyeveti pUrvaH pakShaH, viShNureveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "sarvamAnavirodhashcha' iti, "doShAtyaspR^iShyiniyamaH' ityukttapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyau bAdhyabAdhakabhAvaM darshayan.h vivR^iNoti -
avaratvAdidharmaniyantR^itvaM tattAdAtmyavattvaM cheti dvividhaM hyavaratvAdi | niraniShTho niravadya ityAdi shrutestattaddoShatAdAtmyaspR^iShyiniyamAt.h viShNoH nAmAni sarvANi yamAvishantIti shrutibalAchcha niyantR^itvamavaratvAdikamityApatati ||
|| avaratvAdItyAdinA || siddhAntayukttiM saN^gamayituM tadupayukttaM tAvadAha- avaratvAdidhamarniyantR^itvamiti || (tattAdAtmyamityatra tachChabdenAvarAdivastuparAmarshaH |) avaratvAdItyataH pUrvaM "paragatA' iti sheShaH | avaratvAdiavaratvAdishabdapravR^ittinimittamityarthaH | hishabdaH tasya, "yadadhInA guNA yasya tadguNI so.abhidhIyate' ityAdipramANaprasiddhidyotakaH | nanu, astvevamavarAdishabdapravR^ittinimittadvaividhyam.h; tataH kimityato "neshvarasyAvaratvAdidharmAdhikaraNatvenAvarAdishabdavAchyatvam.h ; yena sarvamAnavirodhaH syAt.h; kintu paragatAvaratvAdidharmaniyantR^itvenaiva' iti vivakShuravaratvAdidharmAdhikaraNatvenAvarAdishabdavAchyatvAbhAve hetutvena sapramANakaM siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- niraniShTha iti || nanu doShAtyaspR^iShTiniyamasya, avarAdishabdavAchyatvAbhAvenApyupapatteravaratvAdiniyantR^itvena tachChabdavAchyatvApAdakatvaM kathamityata ukttam.h - nAmAnIti || nanu, tathApi na paragatAvaratvAdiniyantR^itvenAvarAdishabdavAchyatvaM viShNoH "niraniShThaH' ityAdishruterarthasaN^kochenAvaratvAdyadhikaraNatvenAvarAdishabdavAchyatvasya vA, "nAmAni sarvANi' iti shruterarthasaN^kochenAvarAdishabdavAchyatvasyaiva vA sambhavAt.h ityata Aha- 
shrutidvayasyApi niravakAshatvAt.h | mR^ityushabdAdiShu prasiddheshcha | prasiddhatvAtkartR^ivyutpatteH | tameva mR^ityumamR^itaM, tAta daivaM sarvAtmanA vai hi paraM parAyaNamityAdeshcha | upachArakalpanAyAshcha kliShyatvAt.h | 
|| shrutidvayasyeti || nanu, bhavedetatpradhAnAdigatashabdapravR^ittinimittaprerakatveneshvarasyAvarAdishabdavAchyatvam.h, yadyanyagatapravR^ittinimittaprerako.asau shabdo vartata iti siddhayet.h ; tadeva kutaH ityata Aha- mR^ityushabdAdiShviti || "anyagatamArakatvAdiniyAmakatvena yamAdivAchakatvasya' iti sheShaH | evaM tarhyanyagatapravR^ittinimittaprerake vR^ittiramukhyA syAdityato vAha- mR^ityushabdAdiShviti || mR^ityushabdasya, yamAdivAchakatvasya, prasiddheH bahulaprayogasiddhatvAt.h, bahulaprayogasiddhasya cha mukhyatvAdityarthaH | na kevalamukttanyAyena avarAdishabdavAchyatvaM viShNoH kintu "sa baddhaH' "sa duHkhI' "sa baddhayati' "sa duHkhayati' ityAdishrutiShu baddhAdishabdAnAM viShNau kartR^ivyutpatteH prasiddhatvAchchetyAha- prasiddhatvAditi || smR^itAvapi, viShNau kartR^ivyutpatti (anyagatapravR^ittinimittaniyAmakatva)mapekShya shabdaprayogo.astItyAha- tameveti || mR^ityuM mArakam.h | amR^itaM mochakam.h | nanvatra mR^ityupramukhashabdAnAmaupachArikatvaM kiM nasyAdityata Aha- upachAreti || tarhi "siMho devadattaH' ityatrApi na syAdityata Aha - 
pramANAbhAvAchcha | nAvyakttAdishabdAnAM paramAtmaviShayatvAN^gIkAre sarvamAnavirodhaH || 1 ||
|| pramANAbhAvAditi || tatra mukhyArthabAdhAnusandhAnarUpapramANasadbhAvAdaupachArikatvamatra tu tadabhAvAnnaupachArikatvamiti bhAvaH | siddhAntanyAyaphalatvAtpUrvapakShanyAyaniShedhasya, idAnIM tanniShedhapUrvaM pUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNoti - nAvyakttAdishabdAnAmiti || "avyakttAtpuruShaH paraH' ityAdivAkyagatAvyakttAdishabdAnAM paramAtmavAchakatvAN^gIkAre, puruShagataparatvAvadhitvAdinA avaratvAdiprAptyA, "na tatsamashchAbhyadhikashcha dR^ishyate' ityAdisarvamAnavirodho netyarthaH | tathAcha viShNoravyakttAdishabdavAchyatve.avaratvAdiprAptau sarvamAnavirodhAt.h, pradhAnAdyevAvyakttAdishabdavAchyamiti pUrvapakShe, doShAtyaspR^iShyiniyamAd.h, viShNoravyaktAdiniyAmakatvenAvyakttAdishabdavAchyatvamiti siddhAnta  iti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "tadadhInatvAt.h' ityanena,
avaratvAdiniyAmakatvenaivAvaratvAdishabdajAtamarthavannAvaratvAdyadhikaraNatvena, tathAtve "niraniShThaH' ityAdi sarvamAnavirodhaH ityarthakena sUchitaH | yadvA "tadadhInatvAt.h' ityanenArthavattvasAdhanena shrutinairarthyApAdakatvasUchanena sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyaH tadadhInatvAdityenoktto bhavati |) || 1 || OM jyotirupakramAttu tathA hyadhIyata eke OM || atra "vasante vasante jyotiShA yajeta' itivAkyagatajyotirAdishabdAnAM prAgukttasaMshayabIjena bhagavatparatvakarmAdiparatvakoTikasaMshaye karmAdiparatvameveti pUrvaH pakShaH | bhagavatparatvamiti siddhAntaH | etatpUvarpakShasiddhAntasAdhakatvena "vyutpatterapyashakyatA' iti "shabdAtharAnekatA tathA' iti nyAyau bAdhyabAdhakabhAvaM darshayanvivR^iNoti- 
rUDho rUDhiyogo mahAyogo mahArUDhiyogo rUDhopachAro rUDhalakShaNopachAro lakShaNeti shabdavR^ittibhedAH rUDhipUrvakatvena mahAyogavR^ittyA parameshvare.akhilashabdavyutpatyupapatteH || 2 ||
|| rUDhirityAdinA || shabdArthAnAmanekatvopapAdanArthaM vR^ittibhedakathanam.h | nArAyaNAdishabdAnAM mahArUDhiyogaH, AnandamayAdishabdAnAM mahAyogaH iti bhagavati vR^ittidvayam.h | taditaratra yathAyathamitarAH sapta vR^ittaya iti j~nAtavyam.h | eteShAM lakShaNodAharaNAni tatvaprakAshikAdau draShyavyAni | jyotirvasantastomAdishabdAnAM yAgakAlasamUhAdiShu rUDhatvAt.h , shabdAntarANAM, yogAdisadbhAve.api rUDheH prAyikatvAchcha- rUDhipUrvakatvenetyukttam.h | rUDhyAdipUrvakatvenetyAshayaH | ata eva tatvaprakAshikAyAM "vR^ittIH' iti bahuvachanaprayogenaitadabhiprAya ukttaH | "vyutpattyupapattiH' iti vadataiva "tadashakyatA' ityetadadhikaraNapUrvapakShasAdhiketi vivR^itaM bhavati | (vyutpattyupapattirityupalakShaNam.h | karmAdiphalopalakShaNavirodhAbhAvashchetyapi draShyavyam.h | tena, "ashakyatApi' iti bhinnakrameNApishabdena samuchchitaH karmakramAdiviloparUpo nyAyo vivR^ito draShyavyaH |) tatashcha sarvashabdAnAM brahmaparatve, jyotiShyomAdishabdeShu "jyotiShAM stomaH' iti vigrahe bhagavannAmAvR^ittimAtraprasaN^gAdvayutpatterapyashakyatvena karmAdivAchakatvameva jyotiShyomAdishabdAnAmapi pUrvapakShe, shabdArthAnAmanekatvAjjyotirAdishabdAnAmanyatra rUDhyAdivR^ittyabhyupagamena mahAyogavR^ittyA parameshvare shabdapravR^ittyabhyupagamAjjyotiShAM stoma ityAdyakhilashabdavyutpattyupapatteH, brahmaiva jyotiShyomAdishabdavAchyamiti siddhAnta iti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "kalpanopadeshAt.h' ityatra sUtre.avirodha ityanena sUchitaH | siddhAnte vyutpattyavirodhaM vadatA pUrvapakShe tadashakyatAlakShaNavirodhasUchanAt.h | siddhAntanyAyastu "madhvAdivat.h' ityanena bhAgenokttau bhavati, shabdArthAnekatAyA 
anenokttatvAt.h |) || 2 || OM na saN^khayopasaN^grahAdapi nAnAbhAvAdatirekAchcha OM || "yasminpaJNchapaJNchajanA AkAshashcha tiShThataH' iti vAkyagatapaJNchajanAdishabdAH pUrvokttasandehabIjena viShNorvAchakA na veti sandehe, viShNorvAchakA na bhavantIti pUrvaH pakShaH | viShNovarAchakA iti siddhAntaH | etatpUrvapakShasiddhAntasAdhakatvena "parasparavirodhashcha' iti "bahurUpatvamIshasya' iti ukttau nyAyau pUvarvadeva vivR^iNoti- 
bahurUpatvAdadhikaraNAdheyatvAdi tasyaiva yujyate | vyaktayapekShayA kAraNatvaM cha || 4 || 
|| iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachite shrImannyAyavivaraNe prathamAdhyAyasya chaturthaH pAdaH || 
tasyaiva Ishasyaiva | idaM cha "bahurUpatvAt.h' ityatrApyAkarShaNIyam.h | evakAreNa tasyaikasyaiva, natvanyasAhityeneti vA, atAdR^ishaviruddhadharmaghaTakabahurUpatvAdyaishvaryaM nAnyasyeti vA, abhipraiti | AdheyatvAdikimityAdipadena, IshatvAdheyatvayorekatvabahutvayorgrahaNam.h | tathAcha, "ekasminnAdhArAdheyatvayorekatvabahutvayoH, Ishasya sarvAdhAratvAdIshatvAdheyatvayoshcha parasparaM virodhaH' iti pUrvapakShanyAyo vivR^ito bhavati | evaMcha paJNchajanAdishabdAnAM viShNuvAchakatve, AdhArAdheyatvAdInAM, ekasmin.h parasparavirodhAnna viShNoH paJNchajanAdishabdavAchyatvamiti pUrvapakShe, Ishasya bahurUpatvAdvirodhAprasaN^gAdviShNoreva paJNchajanAdishabdavAchyatvamiti siddhAnta iti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyo "na saN^khayopasaN^grahAt.h' ityanena sUchitaH |) || 3 || OM kAraNatvena chAkAshadiShu yathAvyapadiShyoktteH OM, ityatra, "Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH' iti vAkyagatAkAshAdishabdA ukttabIjenAkAshAdimAtravAchakA, uta viShNorapIti sandehe, AkAshAdereveti pUrvaH pakShaH, viShNorapIti siddhAntaH | etatpUrvapakShasiddhAntasambandhitvena "virodhaH kArya tadvatoH' iti, "Ishasya vyaktayavyakttivisheShitA' iti nyAyau pUrvavadeva vivR^iNoti - 
vyakttapekShayA iti || adhyaktayapekShayetyapi j~nAtavyam.h | chashabdaH kAraNatvasamuchchayAtharo, "yujyata' ityasyAnukarShaNArthashcha j~nAtavyaH | "tasyaiva' ityasyobhayatrAnuvR^ittiH | "yujyata' ityetadanukarShaH | ekasyaiva kAryakAraNabhAvAnupapattiretatpUrvapakShasAdhiketi "virodhaH kAryatadvatoH' iti nyAyo vivR^ito bhavati | tathAcha AkAshavAyvAdishabAdavAchyatve, viShNoH kAraNatvaprAptiH | kAryakAraNayorekatvasya virodhAt.h bhUtAkAshAdyevAkAshAdishabdavAchyamiti pUrvapakShe, vyattayavyakttivisheShatvAdIshvarasya kAryakAraNabhAvopapatterviShNurAkAshAdishabdavAchya iti siddhAnta iti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH, kAryatve sati kAraNatvarUpAvAntarakAraNatvArthaka "kAraNatvena cha' ityanena sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyastu, "AkAshAdiShu' ityanena, AkAshAdiShu sthitasya paramAtmano vyaktayavyaktayapekShayA kAryakAraNabhAvamupapAdayatokttaH |) || 4 || OM dR^iShyAntAnuparodhAt.h OM ityadhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntasambandhinau "strIliN^gatvam.h' iti "utpAdanaM svadehAchcha' iti nyAyau bhAShya eva spaShyapratibhAsatvAdatra na vivR^itau | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "sAkShAchchobhayAmnAnAt.h' iti sUtreNa hareH strIliN^gashabdavAchyatvamupapAdayatA sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyastu "yonishcha hi gIyate' ityanenokttaH |) OM etena sarve vyAkhyAtAH OM ityatrApi adhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntasambandhinau "niSheShashcha' iti "durjanAvyakttatA' iti nyAyau bhAShya eva spaShyaM pratipAditatvAnneha vivR^itAviti | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "etena' ityanena sUchitaH, tena niShedhAdInAM bhagavadadhInatvoktteH | siddhAntanyAyastu "vyAkhyAtAH' ityanena sUchitaH | niShedhyalakShaNapravR^ittinimittAbhAve.api harau durjanAvyakttatvAdinA shUnyAdishabdA vyAkhyAtAH - ityarthatvAttasya |) || 5-7 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNabhAvabodhe shrIraghUttamayatikR^ite prathamAdhyAyaH || 
AnandamayAdyupalakShitAsheShavaidikashabdasamanvayena siddhe jagajjanmAdikAraNatvAdau prathamAdhyAyArthe, yuktayAdivirodhaparihArAtharmayaM dvitIyo.adhyAyaH pravR^ittaH | tatra sarvavirodhAnAM yukttimUlakatvAdyukttereva prAdhAnyAttadvirodhaparihArArtho.ayaM prathamaH pAdaH pravR^ittaH | etatpAdIyAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAH saN^graheNAnuvyAkhyAyAmukttAH | "AptatA samatA.adR^iShyishrutisAdhyabalodbhavAH | sarvAnusAro laghutA visheShAdarshanA.aphale | iShyAsiddhishcha niyamaH pUrvapakSheShu yukttayaH | etA eva tvatibalAH siddhAntasya niyAmakAH' iti || OM smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^ga iti chennyasmR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^gAt.h OM, ityatra matamivamatyA jagajjanmAdikartR^itvaM viShNoryukttaM, na veti sandehe na yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "AptatA' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasiddhAntobhayasambandhitvena vivR^iNoti-
rudrAdInAM sakAshAdviShNvAdInAmevAptatvam.h | shrutyanusAritvAt.h || 1 || na shruteH rudrAdismR^itisAmyaM kintu sAkShipratyakShasAmyameva 
nirapekShatvAt.h || 2 ||
|| rudrAdInAmiti || anena rudrAdInAmAptatvaM pUrvapakShanyAyaH iti sUchitaM bhavati | tathAcha rudrAdInAM jagaddhitopadeShyR^itvena sarvaj~natvena vAkyAtharj~nAnAdimattvarUpAptatAvattvAt.h, tadvirachitAnAM smR^itInAM doShAbhAvaguNayukttatayA prabalatvena niravakAshatvAttadviruddhAbhidhAyakashruterapramANyasyaiva prasaN^gAnna tayA viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM siddhayatIti pUrvaH pakSha iti bhAvaH | ""viShNvAdInAmeva' ityevakAreNa siddhAntayuktteH prAbalyamAha- tatra hetumAha- shrutIti || viShNvAdivirachitasmR^itInAmiti sheShaH | atra shrutyanusAro nAma yathAtathaM tatsaMvAdastanmUlatvaM cheti dvayamapi grAhyam.h | anena pAshupatAdishrutInAM shrutivirodhenApyaprAmANyamukttaM bhavati | tathAcha vaiShNavasmR^itInAM paramAptairviShNvAdibhiH praNItatvena niravakAshatvAt.h pAshupatAdismR^itInAM tadvirodha evAprAmANyaprasaN^gAt.h sutarAM tatsAhAyyavatA shrutyA virodhe.aprAmANyaprasaN^ga iti yukttameva viShNorjagatkartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH, "smR^ityanavakAshaH' sati sautrapUrvabhAgena pAshupAdismR^itInAM anavakAshamApAdayatA sUchitaH | rudrAderAptatvaM vinA tatsmR^ityanavakAshatvAnirvAhAt.h | anyatheShyApAdanaM syAt.h | "itareShAM chAnupalabdheH' iti dvitIyasUtreNa niShedhyatayA sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyastu "smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^gAd.h' iti siddhAntAMshena sUchitaH |) || 1 || OM na vilakShaNatvAdasya tathAtvaM cha shabdAt.h OM ityatra pramANApramANabhUtavAkyopalabdhyA shrutyAdikaM pramANaM na veti sandehe, na pramANamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, pramANameveti siddhAntaH | tatra "samatA' ityanenokttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvan.h pratikShipati || nashruteriti ||  yathAvidyamAnArthAbhidhAyakatvena rudrAdivirachitapAshupatAdismR^itInAmaprAmANyaM, tathA "kArIryA yajeta vR^iShyikAmaH' iti shruteH | upalakShaNametat.h | paJNcharAtrAdismR^iteshcha | kArIryAdyanuShThAne.api vR^iShyayAdyadR^iShyayA.avidyamAnArthAbhidhAyakatvAdaprAmANyamityevaM rUpaM shruteH rudrAdismR^itisAmyamiti na tayA viShNorjagatkartR^itvaM siddhayatIti netyarthaH | taddhetutvena "samatA' ityanenaivokttanyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvena vivR^iNoti- kintviti || yathA sAkShipratyakShasya prAmANyaM niyataM, tathA shruteH paJNcharAtrAdismR^iteshcha prAmANyaM niyatam.h | prAmANyaniyamapradarshanArthameva sAkShItyukttam.h | evakAreNa rudrAdismR^itisAmyaM vyAvartayati | atra hetumAha- nirapekShatvAditi || kartR^iguNapramANAntarasaMvAdaphalasaMvAdAdyapekShashUnyatvAdityarthaH | ayaM bhAvaH | vAkyAprAmANyaM vakttR^idoShanibandhanam.h ; nahi nitye vede doShAH kalpayituM shakyante | ato nityatvAdadoShavAkyatvenAnyAnapekShitatayA sAkShipratyakShatvaprAmANyamiti | shrutyapekShayaivaitat.h | paJNcharAtrAdismR^itestu shrutirUpapramANAnukUlatvahetunA sarvametadupapAdanIyam.h | tathAcha, AshvAsasambhavAchChrutyAdyukttaM jagatkartR^itvaM viShNoryukttamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "tathAtvam.h' ityanenoktto bhavati | siddhAntanyAyAshcha vilakShaNatvAd.h' ityaMshena sUchito bhavati, shrutyAdernityatvAt.h nirdoShatvAdilakShaNasya sAkShipratyakShasAmyasya sUchanAt.h |) || 2 || OM abhimAnivyapadeshastu visheShAnugatibhyAm.h OM ityatra sandehatadbIjapUrvapakShasiddhAntAH pUrvAdhikaraNavadeva draShyavyAH | tatra, "adR^iShyiH' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitayA tatphalaM sUchayanvivR^iNvan pratikShipati - 
na mR^idAdInAM vachanAdyadR^iShyiH shrutyaprAmANyakAraNam.h | 
|| na mR^idAdInAmiti || pratyakShAdisiddhamR^ijjalatejaHprabhR^itInAM, "vachanAdyadR^iShyiH' ityasya, "vachanekShaNAdyadR^iShyiH' iti, naJNvyatyAsena "vachanekShaNAdyabhAvadR^iShyiH' iti chArthaH | anena dR^iShyAnte sAdhyasattvaM pradarshitam.h | mR^idAdInAmityanenaiva mR^idAditvaM, jaDatvaM cha sAdhanaM pradarshitam.h | tathAcha prasiddhamR^idAdau, jaDatvAderhetoH, vakttR^itvAdyabhAvena, vyAptirityukttaM bhavati | evaMcha jaDatvAdihetorAdikAlInamR^idAdirUpapakShadharmatvaM cha draShyavyam.h | tatashcheyaM mR^idAdInAM vachanAdyadR^iShyiH, naJNvyatyAsena vyAptidR^iShyatvena, "sargAdyakAlInamR^idAdikaM vakttR^itvAdyupetaM na bhavati, jaDatvAt.h ; prasiddhamR^idAdivat.h' ityanumAnotthApakatayA, "mR^idabravIt.h'"Apo.abruvan.h' "tA Apa aikShanta' "tatteja aikShata' "oShadhayaH saMvadante' ityAdishruteraprAmANyakAraNam.h | ato vishvasAbhAvAnna tayA jagatkartR^itvaM siddhayatIti bhAvaH | kathaM tarhi, niravakAshatvenokttaprabalAnumAnavirodhaparihAraH shruterityAshayavAn.h pR^ichChati- 
api tu vachanAdishakttAyA devatAyA mR^idAdishabdavAchyatvadyotikaiva || 3 || Ishvarasya sraShyR^itvavadasato.api sraShyR^itvaM shrUyata iti nAsti |
|| api tviti || taduttaratvane "adR^iShyiH' ityanenaivokttanyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitayA vivR^iNoti- vachanAditi || AdipadenekShaNAdikaM grAhyam.h | shakttAyAH ityanena vakttR^itvAdyupayukttavigrahAderapi dyotyatvaM sUchayati- dyautikaivetyavadhAraNena 
pUrvapakShaM vyAvartayati | nanu, mR^idAdInAM vachanAdyadR^iShyeH, "mR^idabravIt.h' ityAdivedAprAmANyenApyupapatteH kathaM vachanAdishakttadevatAyA mR^idAdishabdavAchyatvadyotakatvamavadhAryate iti chenna, vedasya nidoShavAkyatvena aprAmANyAbhAvasya nishchitatvAdityasyApyevakAreNokttatvAditi | ata evokttaM tatvaprakAshikAyAM - "achetanasya vachanAdyadR^iShyayA, nirdoShavAkyasyAprAmANyAdR^iShyayA cha tatkalpanopapatteH' iti | tathAcha shrutyukttaM jagatkAraNatvaM viShNoryukttameveti bhAvaH | (atrAchetanasya vachanAdyadR^iShyayA, nirdoShavAkyasyAprAmANyAdR^iShyayA cha abhimAnivyapadeshaM samatharyatA "abhimAnivyapadeshastu' iti sUtreNa, achetanasya vachanAdyadR^iShyiH pUrvapakShanyAyaH, nirdoShavAkyasyAprAmANyAdR^iShyiH siddhAntanyAyaH iti sUchitamiti j~nAtavyam.h |) || 3 || OM asaditi chenna pratiShedhamAtratvAt.h OM || ityatra "yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante' "asadevedamagra AsIt.h' iti shrutivipratipattyA jagatkAraNatvaM viShNoryukttamayukttaM veti sandehe, na viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti siddhAntaH | tatra "shrutisAmyam.h' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati - Ishvarasyeti || yatheshvarasya sraShyR^itvaM "yato vA imAni--' ityAdinA shrUyate, asato.api sraShyR^itvaM "asadevedamagra AsIt.h' ityAdinA shrUyate | tathAcha brahmA.asatoH sraShyR^itvashrutisAmyam.h | ato jagatkAraNatvanishchayaH ityetannAstItyarthaH | kuto na sAmyamityataH "shrutisAmyam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvena vivR^iNoti- 
so.asachChabdo brahmashabdavadeva brahmavAchaka iti shruteH sAmyam.h || 4 || 
so.asachChabda iti || yathA brahmashabdaH "atha kasmAduchyate brahmeti bR^ihanto hyasmin.h guNAH' iti shrutibalAdbrahmavAchakaH, evaM, "tadvA etadAsIdityAha nahyAsAdayati kashchana' iti shrutibalAt.h "asadeva' iti shrutigatA.asachChabdo brahmavAchakaH iti hetoH "asadeva' iti shruteH "yato vA--' iti shrutyA sAmyamekArthapratipAdakatvamityarthaH | anena, shrutisAmyamityetat.h nirvachanashrutyoH, brahmasachChabdayoH, tadupetashrutivAkyayoshcha sAmyamiti tredhA vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | atra, pUrvapakShe, "sato.api' iti apipadena "Ishvarasya' ityukttasamuchchayAt.h "etena shiShyA aparigrahA api--' iti sUtranirasanIyajIvAderapi samuchchayaH | siddhAnte, "asachChabdaH' iti jIvashabda ityAderupalakShaka iti j~nAtavyam.h | tathAcha saN^kShepe- "asajjIvapradhAnAdishabdA brahmaiva nAparam.h | vadanti kAraNatvena--' ityukttam.h | tathAcha shrutyukttaM jagatkAraNatvaM viShNoryukttameveti bhAvaH | (atra, pUrvapakShanyAyo "yato vA--' iti shrutyA brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvavat.h, "asadevedam.h' iti shrutyA asato.api jagatkAraNatvamiti pratipAdakena "asaditi chet.h' iti (sUtra) bhAgena sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha, "pratiShedhamAtratvAt.h' ityAdisUtre asataH kAraNatvapratikShepAt.h, shruternirarthakatvAyogAt.h' "etena sarve vyAkhyAtAH' ityukttanyAyena, asachChabdasya brahmavAchakatvena, "asadeva' iti, "yato vA' iti shrutyoH sAmyamityarthasUchakaiH sUchitaH |) || 4 || OM bhokttApatteravibhAgashchetsyAllokavat.h OM ityatra, vAdivivAdena jagajjanmAdikartR^itvaM paramAtmano yukttamayukttaM veti sandehe, na yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "balodbhavaH' ityukttanyAyaM pUvarpakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati || 
karmANi vij~nAnamayashcha AtmA pare.avyaye sarva ekIbhavanti iti shrutibalAnnaikyam.h | kintu bhedApAdakamevaitat.h "niraJNjanaH paramaM sAmyamupaiti parAtparaMpurishayaM puruShamupaiti divyam.h iti sannihitavAkyabalAt.h | ekIbhAvashabdastu sannidhye.api bhavati | 
|| karmaNIti || atra, "shrutisAmyaH' ityato buddhayA vivekena "shrutiH' ityanuvartata ityabhipretya, shrutibalAdityukttam.h | anena, shrutibalAt.h, udbhavoj~nAnaM yasya jIveshvaraikyaM pUrvapakShanyAya iti vivR^itaM bhavati | tathAcha jIvAbhinnasyeshvarasya jIve.asambhAvyamAnaM jagatkartR^itvaM na yukttamiti pUrvapakSho, netyarthaH | tarhi, shruteraprAmANyAsambhavAtkA gatirityAshayena pR^ichChati - kintviti || shrutigatimAha- bhedApAdakameveti || evakAreNa pUrvapakShaM vyAvartayati | etat.h shrutivAkyam.h | anena, shrutibalodbhavashabdaH siddhAnte bhedapara iti vivR^itaM bhavati | nanu, pUrvapakShe, "ekIbhavanti' iti balamasti, siddhAnte kiM balamityata Aha- niraJNjana iti || nanu, sannihitaitadvAkyAdapi, "ekIbhavanti' ityekIbhAvashabdasya, vAkyAvayavatvenAntaraN^gatayA prabalatvena, aikyApAdakatvameva "karmANi' iti vAkyasya, na bhedApAdakatvamityata Aha- ekIbhAvashabda iti || sAnnidhyaM sthAnaikyam.h | apishabdena matyaikyasamuchchayaH, svarUpaikyAbhAve.apIti vA | antaraN^gatve.api sAvakAshatvAt.h naikIbhAvashabdaH prabalaH, "niraJNjanaH--' ityAdi sannihitavAkyantu, niravakAshatvAtprabalamiti bhAvaH | (naitatsAvakAshatvaM svotprekShitamityAshayena) sthAnaikyamatyaikyAbhyAmekIbhAvashabdaprayogaM darshayati- ekIbhUteti || evamAntaropapattimuktavA bAhyAmapi tAmAha- yathodakamiti || natu tadeva bhavati | evaM vijAnato muneH vijAnatAM munInAmAtmAdhipatipatirhiraNyagarbho.api mukttaH paramAtmAnaM prApya tAdR^igeva bhavati, kimutA.anya ityarthaH | tathAcha shrutibalodbhavAjjIveshvarayorbhedAjjIve.asambhAvyamAnamapi 
jagatkartR^itvaM viShNau yukttameveti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "karmANi' iti shrutibalAt.h shrutibalAt.h eaikyasiddhiriti vadatA "bhokttApatteravibhAgashchet.h' ityaMshenokttaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha, "yathodakam.h' iti sUchito bhavati |) || 5 || OM tadanyatvamArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH OM || paTAdisR^iShyeH svatantrasAdhanasApekShatvadarshanAt.h, IshvarasR^iShyeralaukikatvAt.h, jagatsR^iShyayAdikaM kiM svatantrasAdhanasApekShaM naveti sandehe, svatantrasAdhanasApekShamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra, "sarvAnusAraH' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- na laukiketi || vyAptinishchayAya vyabhichAranirAsArthaM sarvetikAryavisheShaNam.h | pakShavyAvR^ittyarthaM, pramANapradarshanArthaM cha laukiketi | akartR^itantratvaM, upAdAnAdibhUtapradhAnAdeH, kartR^ibhUtaparamAtmatantratvAbhAvaH ityevaMrUpasarvAnusAraH | tathAcha laukikasavarkAryavat.h, kAryatveneshakR^itakAryamapi svatantrasAdhanasApekShamiti pUrvapakSho netyarthaH | IshvarasR^iShyeH kIdR^iktavaM tarhIti pR^ichChati-
kiM tarhi tadvailakShaNyena sarvakartR^ivilakShaNasarvashakttitvamevAsheShayukttishrutyanusAri | eSha sarveshvaraH ityAdishruteH | yukttimAtrAchChrutiyukttA hi yukttirbalIyasI || 6 || 
|| kiM tarhIti || taduttaratvena "sarvAnusAraH' ityukttameva nyAyaM, siddhAntasambandhitvena vivR^iNoti- tadvailakShaNyeneti || tebhyo laukikasarvakAryebhyo, vailakShaNyena svatantrasAdhanarahitatvAkhyena, sarvakAryakartuH paramAtmanaH, svavyatirikttakuvindakulAlAdisarvakartR^ibhyaH vilakShaNaM sAdhanAntaraniyamanAdisarvashakttitvameva asheShayukttishrutyanusArisarvayukttishrutisiddhamityarthaH | prAdhAnyAchChrutimudAharati- sarveshvara iti || evaM, "paratantro hyapekSheta svatantraH kimapekShate | sAdhanAnAM sAdhanatvaM yataH kiM tasya sAdhanaiH' ityAdismR^ityukttAH paratantratvasvatantratvasAdhanasattAtatpradatvAdiyukttayo.api draShyavyAH | nanu, pUrvapakShayuktterapi, vyAptipakShadharmatopetatvena prAbalyAtkathamevaM nirNaya ityata Aha- yukttimAtrAdIti || aN^gIkR^itya chedamuditam.h | bAdhitaviShayatvena pUrvapakShayuktteyarukttitvameva nAstIti j~nAtavyam.h | evaMcha sarvashrutiyuktayanusArAdIshakR^itakAryaM na svatantrasAdhanApekShamiti bhAvaH | (atra, pUrvapakShanyAyo "yathA prANAdiH' ityanena niShedhyatayA sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha, svarapasAmarthyAdeva sraShyR^itvamanekashrutiyuktyanusArItyarthakena "ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH' ityanena sUchitaH |)|| 6 || OM itaravyapadeshAddhitAkaraNAdidoShaprasakttiH OM || ityatra, shrutivipratipattyA, shrutyanubhavavipratipattyA vA, jagatkatarR^itvAdi viShNoryukttamayukttaM veti saMshaye, na yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti  siddhAntaH | tatra "laghutA' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacheshvaratyAgena jIvasyaiva kartR^itvAN^gIkAre kalpanAlAghavam.h | shrutisiddhatvenAkalpanAt.h | ashrutajIvakartR^itvAN^gIkAre gauravameva | 
|| nacheshvaratyAgeneti || tadanaN^gIkAreNetyarthaH | jIvasyaiva, mahadAdikArya iti sheShaH | yadvA, Ishvarasya ghaTAdikartR^itvatyAgenetyarthaH | jIvasyaiva, ghaTAdikArya iti sheShaH | idamukttaM bhavati, neshvarasya mahadAdisakalakAryakartR^itvaM yukttam.h, anupalabdhibAdhimIshvaraM kalpayitvA, tasya sarvakartR^itvakalpane, kalpanAgauravApatteH | IshvarAnaN^gIkAreNa jIvasyaiva sarvakartR^itvAN^gIkAre, kalpanAlAghavam.h | dharmikalpanAto dharmakalpanAyA laghutvAt.h | jIvasya ghaTAdau kartR^itvasya klR^iptatvAchcha | atha devAdivadadR^ishyatvashakttiyogAdanupalabhyamAno.apIshvaraH pramANenAN^gIkriyata iti chet.h, tathApi tasya mahadAdikArya eva kartR^itvamastu, na ghaTAdAvapi | ubhayatra kalpane gauravApatteH | ghaTAdau tu, IshvaratyAgena jIvasyaiva kartR^itvAN^gIkAre, kalpanAlAghavam.h, iti | etachcha netyarthaH | kuto netyato "laghutA' ityukttameva nyAyaM, siddhAntasambandhitvena vivR^iNoti- shrutisiddhatveneti || Ishvarasya, tasya ghaTAdisarvakAryakartR^itvasya chetyarthaH | kalpanA.anekatve khalu kalpanAgauravam.h | Ishvarasya, tasya ghaTAdisarvakAryakartR^itvasya cha shrutisiddhatvena, kalpanAyA evAbhAvAnnobhayapakShoktagauravamiti bhAvaH | tarhi pakShadvayasyApi prAmANikatvena kathaM nirNaya ityata Aha- ashruteti || aN^gIkAra eveti sambandhaH | jIvasya ananyAdhInatayA mahadAdau ghaTAdau vA kartR^itvasya ashrutatvena, tadaN^gIkAra eva gauravam.h, natu Ishvarasya tadaN^gIkAra ityarthaH | tathAcha viparItalAghavamiti vadan.h, nyAyaM vivR^iNoti - 
tadabhAve siddhAnte laghutA | nAnyaH kartA sahi svatantraH paramAtparamo harirityAdeshcha | abhedapakShastu nirAkR^itaH | shrutyanubhavavirodhAchcha || 7 || 
|| tadabhAva iti || IshvarakartR^itvasya shrutisiddhatvenAshrutatvAbhAvAtsiddhAnte, IshvarakartR^itvapakShe laghutetyarthaH | na kevalaM 
jIvakartR^itvasyAshrutatvam.h, tadabhAvAshcha shruta ityabhipretya, tAM shrutimudAharati- nAnya iti || "sa hi' ityAdishrutisheShodAharaNaM, shrutisiddhatvenetyetadupapAdanArtham.h | anyo jIvaH, svAtanteNa sarvakAryANAM na katarA, hi yasmAt.h, tasmAtprasiddho hariH svatantraH anyApreryatayA sarvakAryakartA, paramAtparamaH uttamAduttamaH, iti shrutyarthaH | nanu, shrutirIshvarasya svAtanteNa kartR^itvaM pratipAdayati | "ahaM karomi' ityAdyanubhavastu, jIvasya tathAkartR^itvaM gocharayati | nacha svatantravastudvayamaN^gIkartaM shakyam.h | tathAtve doShasya vakShyamANatvAt.h | ataH shrutyanubhavAnyatAnupapattyA jIveshvarayorabhedAN^gIkAre, jIvapakShasyApi shrautatvAnna kalpanAgauravamityata Aha- abhedapakShastviti || nirAkR^ito "bhokttR^iApatteH' ityAdAviti bhAvaH | anubhavasya parAdhInAlpakartR^itvaviShayatvaM, bhrAntitvaM veti bhAvaH | pramANAntaravirodhAchcha nAbhedapakSho yuktta ityAha- shrutIti || evaMcha prAmANikapakShasyaiva laghutayA, IshvarakartR^itvasya shrutisiddhatvAt.h, yukttameveshvarasya kartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra, pUvarpakShanyAyaH "upasaMhAradarshanAnneti chet.h' ityanena, jIvakatarR^itve pratyakShasadbhAvoktayA sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha, "devAdivadapi' iti sUtre, shruteryogyAnupalambhabAdhaparihAreNa, shrutisiddhAntatvasUchanAtsUchitaH |) || 7 || OM shrutestu shabdamUlatvAt.h OM || ityatra, Ishvarasya jagatkartR^itve tatra tatroktanyAyaiH, kR^itsnaprasaktyAdidoShaishcha jagatsraShyR^itvaM viShNoryukttaM veti sandehe, na yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "visheShAdarshanam.h' ityukttanyAyaM, siddhAntasambandhitvena tAvadvivR^iNoti-
shabdaikasamadhigamyatvasarvashakttitvAdInAM visheShANAmadarshanaM jIve | na jIvAdvisheShAdarshanaM parameshvare | visheShashrutereva || 8 ||  
|| shabdaikasamadhigamyatveti || shabdaikasamadhigamyatvaM, "shabdamUlatvAt.h' iti sUtrokttam.h, sarvashakttitvAdayastu, "Atmani chaivaM vichitrAshcha hi' ityAdisUtrokttAH | eteShAM visheShANAM jIve.adarshanam.h | atra darshanashabdo j~nAnamAtraparaH | j~nApakashrutyAdirUpapramANAbhavAditi bhAvaH | siddhAntaphalatvAtpUrvapakShaniShedhasyedAnIM "visheShAdarshanam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM, pUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati - na jIvAditi || parameshvare, jIvAdvisheShANAM jIvavyAvartakAnAM, tatrAvidyamAnAnAmiti yAvat.h | kR^itsnaprasaktayAdidoShanirAsakAnAmadarshanaM netyarthaH | adarshanAbhAvo darshanam.h | tatkena pramANenetyAkAN^kShAyAmAha- visheShashrutereveti || "na vedavinmanute taM bR^ihantam.h' "vichitrashaktiH puruShaH purANaH' ityAdishruteH, shabdaikasamadhigamyatvasarvashakttitvAdInAM jIvavisheShANAM darshanenAdarshanaM netyarthaH | evakAreNa shruteH prasiddhatAmAha | evaMcha jIvavadIshvare.api kR^itsnaprasaktayAdidoShanirAsakavisheShANAmadarshanAjjagatkartR^itvAyoga iti pUrvapakShe, IshvaragatashabdaikasamadhigamyatvAdivisheShANAM jIve.adarshanAnna jIvasAmyamiti, Ishvarasya jagatkartR^itvaM yukttameveti siddhAnta iti bhAvaH | (atra, pUrvapakShanyAyaH, "shabdamUlatvAt.h' "Atmani chaivaM vichitrAshcha hi' iti sUtradvayena (pUrvapakSha)nirasanIyatayA sUchito bhavati | siddhAntanyAyashcha, avadhAraNArthena "Atmani cha' iti chashabdena, "svapakShadoShAchcha' ityanena cha yukttivirodhaparihAropayogino visheShasya jIve.adarshanoktyA sUchitaH | ) || 8 || OM na prayojanavattvAt.h OM || ityatra, jagatkartR^itvopapAdanAphalAbhyAM, jagatkartR^itvamIshvarasya yukttamayukttaM veti sandehe, na yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti siddhAntaH | tatra "aphalam.h' ityukttanyAyaM, tatphalapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShepati - 
nacha prayojanAbhAvo.akartR^itve kAraNam.h | asheShakartR^itvApAdakashcha | phalApekShiNastvapUrNatvAdeva | na sarvakartR^itvAdishakttiH itarasya pUrNatvAdevAnantashiAkttatvAllIlayaiva kartR^itvam.h || 9 || 
|| nacha prayojanAbhAva iti || tathAcha prayojanAbhAve, pravR^itterevAdR^iShyatvena tasyAkartR^itve kAraNatvAt.h, yadIshvarasya, "na prayojanavattvAt.h' iti prayojanAbhAvo.apyupeyate, tarhi kartR^itvameva na syAt.h, kutaH sarvakartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | kuta ityAkAN^kShAyAM "aphalam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitayA vivR^iNoti- asheSheti || cho hetau | yasmAtprayojanAbhAvaH, asheShakartR^itvApAdakaH, tasmAdakartR^itve kAraNaM na | na kevalaM prayojanAbhAvo.akatarR^itve na kAraNam.h, kintu, asheShakartR^itvApAdakasamuchchayavAchakashchashabdaH | kathaM phalAbhAvo.asheShakartR^itvApAdaka ityata Aha- phalApekShiNastviti || itarasya phalApekShArahitasya | kartR^itvaM asheShakartR^itvam.h | idamukttaM bhavati | IshvaraH asheShakatarA, anantakartR^itvAt.h vyatirekeNa devadattavat.h iti | nacha svarUpAsiddhiH Ishvaro.anantashakttiH, pUrNatvAt.h iti tatsAdhanAt.h | nacha vyAptyabhAvaH, apUrNasya sarvakartR^itvAdishaktayabhAvadasharnena, vyatirekavyAptisattvAt.h | nacha tatrApyasiddhiH, phalApekShiNo.apUrNatvaniyamena, phalApekShAshUnyachetanatvapUrNatvasyApi sAdhanAt.h sati prayojanAbhAvaH paramparayAsheShakartR^itvasyApAdaka iti | bhagavataH prayojanAnuddeshe, kIdR^ishI pravR^ittiriti prashnaparihArAya lIlayaivetyukttam.h | nahi lIlA prayojanAya bhavati | aphalarUpanyAyasya pUrvottarapakShaphalasambandho mUla eva spaShyaH | (atra pUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAvanenaiva sUtreNokttau |) | 9 || OM vaiShamyanairghR^iNye na 
sApekShatvAttathA hi darshayati OM || ityatra, jagatkartR^itvAdiviShaye, shrutyA, vaiShamyAdivirodhadarshanena cha jagajjanmAdikartR^itvamIshvarasya yukttamayukttaM veti sandehe, na yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "iShyAsiddhiH' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitayA vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
neshasya pUrNatvAsiddhiH | karmasApekShatvenIshatvamanapekShatve shruteraprAmANyamiti | 
|| neshasyeti || pUrNatvaM, pUrNakartR^itvam.h, asheShakartR^itvamiti yAvat.h | yukttivirodhAditi bhAvaH | anena, iShyasya asheShakartR^itvasya, asiddhiriti nyAyo vivR^ito bhavati | kuta IshasyAsheShakatarR^itvaM yukttiviruddhamiti chet.h, "IshvaraH kiM tatprANikarmasApekShaH san.h sukhaduHkhAdi sarvaM karoti, uta tannirapekShaH' iti vikalpaM manasi nidhAya, Adye doShamAha - karmasApekShatva iti || atra, nirnimittaM prANinAM sukhaduHkhAdidAnena vaiShamyanaigharR^iNye syAtAmityapi grAhyam.h | yadIshvaraH karmAnapekShayA phalAdipradAtA, tarhi jyotiShyomayAgAdeH svargAdisAdhanatvaM na syAt.h, tadabhAve.api bhagavatastatkAryatvAyogAt.h | tathAcha, "jyotiShyomena svargakAmo yajeta' ityAdishruteraprAmANyaM syAdityarthaH | ato netyataH, "iShyAsiddhiH' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitayA vivarituM, karmasApekShatvamabhyupetya, tatrokttadoShaparihArArthamAha- 
karmaNo.api tadadhInatvam.h | tathApi tadanusAreNa phaladAnamityanaN^gIkAra eveShyashrutiprAmANyAsiddhiH || 10 || 
|| karmaNopIti || na kevalaM phalAdeH, kintu karmaNo.api ityapishabdArthaH | tathAchApekShyakarmaNo.api svAdhInatvAt.h nAnIshatvamiti bhAvaH | nanu, svaniyamyApekShA nAmAnapekShyaiva, tathAcha, kimIshvaraH kartA karmApekShya karotItyaN^gIkAryam.h ityato nyAyaM vivR^iNoti- tathA.apIti || yadyapi, karmaNastadadhInatvena tadapekShA nAmAnapekShaiveti sheShaH | tadanusAreNa karmAnusAreNa, phalasya shubhAshubhalakShaNasyeshvarakartR^ikadAnamityanaN^gIkAra eva iShyasya "jyotiShyomena svagarkAmo yajeta' ityAdishrutiprAmANyasyAsiddhiH, natu tathAN^gIkAra ityarthaH | tathAcheshvarasya karmAnapekShashrutiprAmANyarUpeShyAsiddheH, karmApekShA | tatashcha na vaiShamyAdidoShaH | apekShyakarmaNashcheshAdhInatvAt.h neshatvAsiddhidoSho.apIti, yukttamIshvarasya savarjagatkartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyo "vaiShamyanairghR^iNye na' ityanena sUchitaH | yadvA, "upapadyate chApyupalabhyate cha' iti sUtreNa pakShadvaye.api doShaparihArAt.h "karmApekShatve, asvAtantyam.h, karmanirapekShatve vaiShamyAdyApAtaH' iti sUchanena sUchito bhavati | siddhAntanyAyashcha "upalabhyate cha' ityanena vedAprAmANyakAraNasya vaiShamyAderupalabhyamAnatvAditi pratipAdayatA sUchitaH |) || 10 || OM sarvadharmopapatteshcha OM || ityatra, samanvayAddhayAyAnyatrAdarshanAbhyAM, pUrNatvaM viShNoryukttamayukttaM veti sandehe, na yukttamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttameveti siddhAntaH | tatra "niyamaH' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitayA vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
sarvachetanA apUrNaguNA iti niyamo na | svatantrasya pUNarguNatvaniyamAt.h | "aiapUrNo.ayaM jIvasaN^gho.asvatantraH pUNaro hariryaH svatantraH sadaiva | nahi svatantro.apUrNatAM kAmayati, pUrNo yadi syAdasvatantraH kutaH saH || iti shruteH || 11 || 
|| iti dvitIyAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 
|| sarvachetanA iti || ata eva vyabhichArashaN^kAparihArArthaM sarvetyukttam.h | tathAcheshvarasyApi chetanatvenApUrNatayA avashyambhAvitvAnna jagatkartR^itvaM yukttamiti pUrvapakSho netyarthaH | kuto netyato "niyamaH' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvena vivR^iNoti- svatantrasyeti || svatantrasya pUrNaguNatvena vyAptirityarthaH | anena pUrvapakShyukttAnumAne, asvAtantyamupAdhirityapi sUchitam.h | nanvevaM, satpratipakShatvenAnirNayaH syAditi chenna, asmadukttAnumAnasya shrutisiddhavyAptipakShadharmatopetatvena prabalatvAt.h, iti bhAvena tatpratipAdakashrutimudAharati - apUrNo.ayamiti || anenAnumAne vyatirekavyAptiH, upAdhAvanvayavyAptirukttA bhavati | ayamityapUrNatvasya jIve.anubhavasiddhatAmAha | evaM vyAptimuktavA pakShadharmatApradarshanapUrvakaM pratij~nAM darshayati | anena, "hariH pUrNaH, svatantratvAt.h' iti prayoga uktto bhavati | yachChabdena hareH pUrNatvasvAtantyayoH shrutiprasiddhimAha- sadaiveti || svAtantAderanAgantukatvamukttam.h | apUrNasyAsvAtanteNa vyAptyanaN^gIkAre bAdhakamAha- nahIti || hi yasmAt.h, svatantraH svasyApUrNatAM na kAmayIta, tataH pUrNa ityarthaH | idAnImasvAtantyasyApUrNatvena vyAptimupapAdayati- pUrNa iti || saH jIva iti sambandhena, bhAvaH | (atra, pUrvapakShanyAyaH "upapatteH' ityanena, sarvachetanAnAmapUrNatvaniyamAtparamAtmano.api chetanatvAtpUrNatvasyAnupapattiriti sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha shrutisUchakena samuchchAyakachashabdena svAtantAdilakShaNayuktteH sUchanAt.h svAtantAdimataH pUrNatvaniyama iti sUchanena sUchitaH | tadukttaM tatvaprakAshikAyAm.h- na kevalaM yuktayA sarvadharmopapattiH, kintu "guNAH shrutAH' iti sarvadharmopapAdakashruteshcheti bhAvaH iti |) || 11 || 
|| iti dvitIyAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 
ukttavirodhinastattatsamayasiddhAH pUrvapakShanyAyAH tadvirodhino.anye iti prasiddhA eva || 1 || 
|| iti dvitIyAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH || 
samayapAdIyAtradakaraNAnAM sarveShAmanuvyAkhyAne vyAkhyAtatvAt.h, na tatpUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAH saN^graheNokttAH | yadyapi saN^graheNoktayabhAve.api nyAyAnAM prathamAdhyAyagatAdyapAdadvaye vivaraNaM kR^itam.h, tathApyetatpAdIyAdhikaraNeShu nyAyAnAM spaShyamuktatvAdvivaraNaM na kR^itamityAshayenAha- ukttavirodhina iti || ukttajagatkAraNatvAdau, virodhino viruddhArthasAdhakAH; tattatsamayasiddhAH sAN^khayachArvAkAdisiddhAntotprekShitAH, pUrvapakShanyAyAH, tadvirodhinaH, tatsAdhyaviruddhArthasAdhakAH, anye siddhAntanyAyAH | itishabdaH prakArArthaH | tatashchokttavirodhitvena prakAreNa pUrvapakShanyAyAH, tadvirodhitvena prakAreNa siddhAntanyAyAH, anuvyAkhyAne prakarSheNa siddhA eva, natu vivaraNamarhantItyatharH |
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNe bhAvabodhe dvitIyAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH || 
viShNorjagatkAraNatvAdau, adhibhUtAdiviShayashrutInAM parasparavirodhaparihArAyAyaM tR^itIyaH pAdaH pravR^ittaH | etatpAdIyAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAH, anuvyAkhyAyAM saN^graheNokttAH "anubhUtiyukttibahuvAgvailomyaM cha tato.adhikam.h | etatsarvaM sataH sAmyaM dvAravaiyarthyameva cha | dR^iShyayuktayanusAritvamukttAnyAtharAvirodhataH | prasiddhanAmasvIkAre bahuvAkyAnuvartitA | lokadR^iShyayanusAritvaM jIvasAmyamanAditA | tatratatra parij~nAnaM guNasAmyashrutI tathA | utpattimattvaM svaguNAnanubhUtyalpakalpane | nAnAshrutishcha vaichityaM yukttayaH pUrvapakShagAH || vyavasthAnupapattishcha svAtantyamanusAritA | mukhyatAshakttimattvaM cha vairUpyaM sarvasaN^grahaH | gatyAdirIshashakttishcha sarvamAnavirodhitA | abhIShyAsiddhisuvyakttI shAstrasiddhirviparyayaH || visheShakAraNaM cheti siddhAntasyaiva sAdhikAH iti | OM na viyadashruteH OM || ityatra "Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH', "anAdirvAyamAkAshaH' iti shrutivipratipattyA, AkAsha utpattimAnnaveti sandehe, viyadanutpattimadeveti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "anubhUtiyukttibahuvAgvailomyam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM, arthAttatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha viyata utpattimattve.anubhUtiyukttibahuvAgvirodho.asti vyavasthA.ayogAt.h | 
|| nacha viyata iti || utpattimattve, aN^gIkR^ita iti sheShaH | avakAsharUpAkAshasyAnutpatteH sAkShyanubhavasiddhatvena tadutpatteranubhavavirodhaH | tathA viyadanutpattimat.h, vibhutvAt.h, sampratipannavadityAdiyukttivirodhaH, "anAdirvAyamAkAshaH' ityAdibahuvAgvirodhashcha | evaMchAnubhUtyAdivirodhenAkAshasyotpattyabhAvAt.h, tadutpattipratipAdakashrutivajjagatkartR^itvashruterapyaprAmANyAt.h, na viShNojargatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti netyarthaH | taddhetutvena "vyavasthA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- vyavastheti || utpattishruterAkAshapadArthasarvaviShayatvasambhavena mukhyArthatvaM, anAdishruteH katipayAkAshapadArthaviShayatvena gauNatvamiti vyayasthAyogAdityarthaH | tAmeva vyavasthAM darshayati-
avakAshamAtrasyAvyAkR^itAtmakatvAdanutpattivachanAnAM tadviShayatvaM utpattivachanAnAmasitavarNabhUtatadabhimAnisharIraviShayatvaM parAdhInavisheShavattvamAtraviShayatvaM cheti vyavasthA | AkAsho nIlimodeti na pradeshaH kathaJNchana | abhAvo hi pradeshasya nahyatrAbhAva ityapi iti paiN^gishruteH || 1 ||  
|| avakAshamAtrasyeti || digrUpAvakAshasyAvyAkR^itAtmakatvena kUTasthatvAt.h "anAdivarA' ityanutpattivachanAnAM tadrUpAvakAshapadArthaikadeshaviShayatvamityanAditvasyAmukhyatvam.h | "Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH' ityAdyutpattivachanAnAM, asitavarNatvenAnumitotpattimadbhUtAkAshatadabhimAnivinAyakotpattimajjaDasharIraviShayatvam.h | tathA, avakAshatadabhimAnibhUtatadabhimAnirUpANAM chaturNAmapyAkAshapadavAchyAnAM parAdhInavisheShavattvamAtrarUpotpattiviShayatvaM cheti vyavasthA | anena, "Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH' ityAdyutpattipratipAdakavAkyagatAkAshashabdasya sarvaviShayatvam.h, sambhUtAdishabdokttotpatterukttaprakAreNa sarvatrAkAshashabdavAchye sattvAt.h | "anAdirvA ayamAkAshaH' ityAdivAkyagatAkAshashabdasya sarvAkAshapadavAchyaviShayatvam.h, bhUte kathamapyasambhavAt.h, tasya svarUpeNAtpatterityukttaM bhavati | bhUtAkAshasyAsitavarNatve shrutimAha- AkAsha iti || nIlimA nIlarUpavishiShyaH | pradeshaH avakAshaH | kathaJNchana svarUpeNa, vikR^itarUpeNa vA, nodetIti sambandhaH | anutpattau yukttimAha- abhAvo hIti || yasya chotpattiH, tasya prAgabhAvena bhAvyam.h | nacha pradeshasya prAgabhAvaH sambhavati | anutpannapratItikatvAditi bhAvaH | tatkathamityata Aha- na hyatreti || apipadena naJNo.anukarShaH | abhAvo hi pratIyamAnaH "asya, atra' iti pratIyate, natu nirAshrayaH | nacha pradeshAbhAvasyAshrayapratItirupapadyate, 
yadeva "atra' iti nirdishyate, tasyaiva pradeshatvAdityarthaH | tathAchAkAshotpattyanutpattishrutyorukttamArgeNa vyavasthopapatteH, prAmANyasambhavAdyukttaM harerviyadAdijagatkatarR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra, pUrvapakShanyAyaH, "gauNyasambhavAt.h' iti sUtreNAnutpattishrutigatiM vadatopalakShaNatvena sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashchAnenaiva sUtreNokttaH |) || 1 || OM etena mAtarishvA vyAkhyAtaH OM || ityatra, "tAsAM vAyurvatsaH sAvA eShA devatAnAdiryo.ayaM pavate' iti vigAnena mukhyo vAyurutpattimAnna veti sandehe, anutpattimAneveti pUrvaH pakShaH, mukhyAvAyurutpattimAneveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "tato.adhikametatsarvam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyamarthAttatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
tato.adhikametatsarvamanubhUtyAdiviruddhatvaM vAyUtpattAviti na vAyoreva mukhyAnutpattyanupapatteH ||
|| tato.adhikamiti || etachChabdaparAmR^iShyaM darshayati- anubhUtyAdiviruddhamiti || Adipadena yukttibahuvAggrahaNam.h | adhikamityenenAbhyadhikAshaN^kAmAha | tathAhi | nachAkAshAnutpattishrutivadvApyanAditvashrutegarauNArthatvam.h | tathA satyAkAshAdivanmukhyavAyorutpattyanutpattimattve, tejo.abannAkAshAdInAM, "atha ha nityAshchAnityAshcha tejo.abannAnyAkAsha iti tAnyanityAni' ityanityatvamuktavA, "vAyurvA va nityaH' iti vAyornityatvokttirayukttA syAt.h | kiMcha vAyoranutpattergauNatvaM nAma svarUpamAtraviShayatvamiti vakttavyam.h | tathA sati tasya sarvachetanasAmyena "atha chetanAshchAchetanAshcha tejo.abannAnyAkAsha iti tAnyachetanAni' iti tejaHprabhR^itInAmachetanatvamuktavA, "vAyurvA va chetanaH' ityukttaM vAyoratishayachetanatvamayukttaM syAt.h | "kuvidaN^gaH' iti R^igukttasarvadevopAsyatA cha notpattimattve ghaTate | tasyodayaniglochAbhAve cha kuto janmasambhavaH | evaMvidhasya chotpattyaN^gIkAre.anubhUtyAdivyAkopaH syAt.h | (tato.adhikametatsarvaM anubhUtiyukttibahuvAgviruddhaM, vAyUtpattAvaN^gIkR^itAyAmityarthaH | ) yukttayashcha "vAyurnotpattimAn.h paramanityatvAt.h, paramachetanatvAt.h, ityAdirUpA draShyavyA | bahuvAchashcha bhAShyodAhR^itA eva | evaM chAnubhUtivirodhena mukhyavAyorutpattyabhAvAd.h vAyUtpattipratipAdakashrutivajjagatkartR^itvashruteraprAmANyAnna viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti netyarthaH | kuto netyatastaddhetutvena "anupapattiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
vAyorevAnutpattyanupapatteH parAdhInavishevattvamAtraM hyutpattiH | tadabhAva ubhayoH svAtantyaM viruddhameva | 
|| vAyoreveti || anutpattishruterbrahmaNyeva mukhyatvAdvAyoranityatvavyApiptavibhakttashakttimattvAchchAnutpatteranupapatterityarthaH | evashabdasya prAbalyAdidyotakatvenAnupapattereveti sambandhaH | yadvA vAyoranutpattiM vadan.h praShyavyaH "kiM vAyurevAnAdiH, Ishvaro.api vA' iti | tatrAdyaM pakShaM dUShayati- vAyoreveti || IshvarAnAditvapratipAdakapramANavirodhena, vAyorevetyanyayogavyavachChedenAnutpatteranupapatterityarthaH | dvitIye, dvayorapi svAtantApAta iti dUShaNamabhipretya tadupapAdayati- parAdhIneti || hi yasmAdvAyorutpattiH parAdhInavisheShalAbharUpA vivakShitA, ataH tadabhAve parAdhInavisheShalAbhAbhAve, ubhayoH vAyuviShNvoH svAtantyaM syAt.h | nacha tadastviti vAchyamityAha- viruddhameveti || ubhayoH svAtantyaM viruddhameva, natu kenApi prakAreNa ghaTanIyamityarthaH | tatkathamityata Aha-

mukhyAnutpattyanupapattiH, dehotpatterapyabhAvAdityAha-
parAdhInavisheShavattvamAtraM tvavyAkR^itakAshasya tadabhimAniprakR^iteshcha samameva || 2 || 
parAdhInavisheSheti || mukhyavAyau parAdhInavisheShavattvamapi mukhyAnutpattyanupapattihetutvena vivakShitam.h, tanmAtraM tu dehAdyutpattirahitayoravakAshachitprakR^ityoshcha samameva | tAdR^ishotpattimAdAya mukhyAnutpattyanupapatteH sattvAdyukttamanupapattervyavasthAprApakatvaM pUrvAdhikaraNe.apIti bhAvaH | yadvA, nanu kimanena, vAyUtpattishrutiH sharIrotpattiviShayA, anutpattishrutirj~nAnaviparItalopaviShayeti vyavasthAN^gIkAreNa, vAyUtpattishrutiH parAdhInavisheShavattvamAtraviShayA, tadanutpattishrutistu dehAdyanutpattiviShayeti vyavasthA kuto nAN^gIkAryA, pUrvAdhikaraNasiddhavyavasthAvilakShaNatvAdityata Aha- parAdhIneti || bhavedevaM yadIyaM vyavasthA pUrvAdhikaraNasiddhavyavasthAvilakShaNA syAt.h | nachaivam.h | bhUtAkAshatadabhimAninoriva pUrvAdhikaraNe.avyAkR^itAkAshatadabhimAninorapi viyachChabdena vivakShitatvAt.h, tayoshcha sharIrAdito.apyutpattyasambhavena parAdhInavisheShavattvamAtreNa vyavasthAyA vAchyatvena, asyAH pUrvAdhikaraNasiddhavyavasthAvailakShaNyAbhAvAt.h | ata evokttaM tadadhikaraNIyatattvaprakAshikAyAm.h- "AkAshapadena bhUtAvakAshataddevatA uchyatante' iti, avakAshatadabhimAninorapyasti parAdhInavisheShalAbhalakShaNotpattiH' iti cha | ata etadadhikaraNavaiyarthyAyokttavidhaiva vyavasthAN^gIkAryaiveti bhAvaH | evaMcha vAyormukhyAnutpattyanupapatteH pUrvavadvayavasthayA shrutiprAmANyasambhavAdyukttaM viShNojargatkAraNatvamiti hR^iyadam.h | (ata pUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAvapyatideshenaiva pUrvAdhikaraNatvasUchitau j~nAtavyau |) || 2 || OM asambhavastu sato.anupapatteH OM || ityatra, "asataH sadajAyata, sadeva somyedamagra AsIt.h' ityAdishrutivibhAgena, brahmotpattimannaveti saMshaye, utpattimadeveti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra (sadeva somyedamagra AsIdityAdishrutivibhAgena) "sataH sAmyam.h' ityuktta pUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha sataH parAdhInavisheShavattvam.h svAtantAt.h || 3 || nacha viShNoreva tejasa utpattau dvArakAraNavaiyarthyam.h | 
|| nacha sata iti || astyeva sataH parabrahmaNaH utpattiH | na chAnAditvashrutivirodhaH | anAditve.apyanAdibhUtayorapi nabhonabhasvatorutpattivat.h, svarUpalAbhAdyutpattyasambhave.api parAdhInavisheShavattvarUpotpattyaN^gIkArAt.h | tathA chotpattimattvenAkAshAdinA sAmyAdbrahmaNo na jagatkartR^itvamiti pUrvaH pakSho netyarthaH | kuto netyatastaddhetutvena "svAtantyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- svAtantAditi || gaganapavanAdInAmasvAtantAdevotpattiriti bhAvaH | evaMcha brahmaNaH svAtanteNAnutpattyupapatternotpattimattvenAkAshAdisAmyamiti yukttaM jagatkAraNatvamiti hR^idayam.h | (atra, pUvarpakShanyAya evashabdArthena tushabdena sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha "sataH' ityanena sUchitaH | ) || 3 || OM tejo.atastathA hyAha OM || ityatra, "vAyoragnistejo.asR^ijata' iti shrutivigAnena, tejaH kiM vAyorjAyate, brahmaNo veti sandehe, vAyoriti pUrvaH pakShaH, brahmaNa iti siddhAntaH | tatra "dvAravaiyarthyam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati - nacha viShNoriti || eveti vAyvapekShArAhityamuchyate | tathAchAyamarthaH | "vAyoragniH' iti shrutiprAmANyanirvAhArthaM tejaso vAyudvArA paramAtmajAtatvaM vadanpraShyavyaH brahma kiM vAyudvAramantareNa sraShyumIShye, naveti | dvitIye, brahmavAyUbhayakAraNatvApattyAdya eva pakShaH svIkAryaH | tatra cha viShNoreva vAyvanapekShayA tejasa utpattAvaN^gIkR^itAyAM vAyurUpadvArakAraNavaiyarthyam.h | tathAcha dvAravaiyarthyAttejaso vAyubrahmobhayakAraNakatvamiti na brahmaNa eva prAdhAnyena kartR^itvamiti netyarthaH | kuto netyatastaddhetutvena "anusAritA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti-

|| dvAramiti || tejaAdikaM prati vAyvAderakAraNatve.api vAyvAdidvAramanusR^ityaiva viShNorichChayaiva lIlayA tejaHprabhR^itisarjanArthaM pravR^itteH shrutyAdisiddhatvAdityarthaH | evaM (cha)shakttatve.api brahmaNaH, shrutisiddhatvena dvArAnusArAdyukttaM sarvakartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyo vAyudvArA tejaso brahmajAtatvamiti siddhAntayatA dvAravaiyarthyAdubhayakAraNatvamiti sUchanena sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha "tathA hyAha' ityanena viShNorvAyudvArA tejaso janakatvamasheShashrutyanusArItyarthakena sUchitaH |) || 4 || OM ApaH OM ityatra, "agnerApastadapo.asR^ijata' iti shrutivigAnena, tejaso.anantaraM prAptA ApaH kiM tejaso jAyante, brahmaNo veti sandehe, tejasa iti pUrvaH pakShaH, brahmaNa iti siddhAntaH | tatra, "dR^iShyayuktayanusAritvam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha tejasa iti || dvArakAraNatvavyAvR^ittyarthaM evashabdaH | tatashcha dvAratAmantareNa, svAtanteNa cha tejasa apAmutpattyaN^gIkAre, dharmAtsvedAdidR^iShyestadanusAritvaM, dR^iShyimUlikA yA, "vimatA Apastejaso jAyante, 
aptvAt.h, svedAdivat.h' iti yukttiH, tadanusAritvamiti hetoH "agnerApaH' iti shruterukttayukttiyukttatvaguNayogena, AdhikyaM prAbalyam.h | yadvA, iti shabdaH prakArArthaH | tadanusAritvamityevaMrUpaguNenAdhikyaM prAbalyamityarthaH | "yuktayanusAritvam.h' iti vakttavye, yat.h "dR^iShyiH' ityukttamanuvyAkhyAne tadabhyadhikAshaN^kApradarshanArtham.h | anyathA "tejo.atastathAhyAha' ityanena nyAyena "agnerApaH' iti shruterapi nirNItatvAnna pUrvapakShotthApakatvam.h | ata eva dR^iShyereva prAdhAnyAdatra dR^iShyayanusAritvAdapAM sAkShAttejojAtatvAnna brahmaNaH sarvakAraNatvamiti cha netyarthaH | kuto netyatastaddhetvena "mukhyataH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
mukhyArthaparityAgaprApteH || 5 ||
|| mukhyArtheti || "idaM sarvamasR^ijata' iti, "kartA sarvasya vai viShNuH' iti shrutismR^itigatasarvashabdasyAsaN^kuchitasarvarUpamukhyArthaparityAgaprApterityarthaH | ukttayuktayupetAyAH "agnerApaH' iti shrutestejaso dvArakAraNatvapratipAdakatvena sAvakAshatvamiti bhAvaH | tatashcha "idaM sarvamasR^ijata' ityAdivAkyagatasarvashabdasya sakalapadArthagrahaNamukhyatAlAbhAtsarvajagatkartR^itvaM viShNoryukttamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyo.api shabdaprayogAdeva sUchitaH | athavA pR^ithagadhikaraNArambhAtsUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha pUrvasUtrAt.h "atastathA hyAha' ityanuvR^ittau satyAM, "sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata' iti shrutipradarshakena "tathA hyAha' ityanena sUchitaH | ) || 5 || OM pR^ithivyadhikArarUpashabdAntarAdibhyaH OM || ityatra, "tA Apa aikShanta bahvayaH syAma prajAyema hIti | tA annamasR^ijanta' "adbhayaH pR^ithivI' iti shrutivigAnenA.apaH kimannasya dvArakAraNamuta pR^ithivyA iti sandehe, nApaH pR^ithivyAH kAraNaM, nApyannasyeti pUrvaH pakShaH, pR^ithivyAH kAraNamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, ukttAnyArthAvirodhataH, prasiddhanAmasvIkAre bahuvAkyAnuvartitA' ityukttaM pUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nachAdbhayo vAnnamutpadyata ityAdyukttaprasiddhAnnAkhyAnyArthAvirodhena prasiddhAnnanAmasvIkAre bahuvAkyAnuvartiteti guNaH | annashabdasya prayogabAhulyAtpR^ithivyAmapi shakttimattvAt.h | 
|| na chAdbhaya iti || "ityAti' ityAdipadena "tA annamasR^ijanta' "tA Apo.annamasR^ijanta' ityAdigrahaNam.h | nApaH pR^ithivyAH kAraNaM, nApyannamayaH, udAhR^itashrutidvayasya parasparaviruddhatvAt.h | niravakAshatvenAnyataragrahaNAyogAt.h | nacha "tA annamasR^ijanta' ityAdishrutigatAnnashabdasya pR^ithivyarthatvena tasyAH sAvakAshatvam.h | "tA annamasR^ijanta' ityAdishrutyukttaH, prasiddharUpo.annAkhyaH, pR^ithivIsakAshAdanyo.atharo yaH, tadavirodhena tadvAchakatveneti yAvat.h, prasiddhasya annamityasya nAmnaH svIkAre, "tasmAdyatra kva cha varShati tadeva bhUyiShThamannaM bhavati' "adbhaya eva taddhayannAdyaM jAyate' ityAdibahuvAkyAnuvartitA, tathA "annamashitaM tredhA vidhIyate' iti prasiddhAnnaliN^gapratipAdakabahuvAkyAnuvartiteti guNalAbhAdityarthaH | upalakShaNametat.h | nApi pR^ithivIshabdasyAnnArthatvena, "adbhayaH pR^ithivI' iti shruteH sAvakAshatA, adbhaya evAnnasR^iShyayaN^gIkAre, "adbhayaH pR^ithivI, pR^ithivyA oShadhayaH, oShadhibhyo.annam.h' iti virodhAt.h ityapi grAhyam.h | evaMcha shrutidvayasyAprAmANyAnna tatsamanvayena viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM siddhayatIti neti bhAvaH | kuto netyatastaddhetutvena "shakttimattvam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- annashabdasyeti || "pR^ithivyAmapi' iti pUrvottarAbhyAM sambadhyate | apipadenAnnasamuchchayaH | "Apashcha pR^ithivI chAnnam.h' "pR^ithivI vA annam.h' "tA Apo.annamasR^ijanta' "pR^ithivI vA annam.h' ityAdishrutAvanna iva pR^ithivyAmapyannashabdasya prayogabAhulyAt.h' prayogabAhulyasya shakttikalpakatvAtpR^ithivyAmannashabdasya shakttimattvAt.h "tA annamasR^ijanta' ityatrAnnashabdena pR^ithivyevochyata ityapAM pR^ithivIM pratyeva dvArakAraNatvamityarthaH | anena "shabdAntarAdibhyaH' iti sautro heturvivR^itaH | annashabdasyobhayatrApi shakttisadbhAvAvisheShAtpR^ithivI(mAtra)paratve ko visheShaheturityataH "adhikArarUpaH' iti sUtrokttaM, "shakttimattvaM cha' ityanuvyAkhyAnagatachashabdokttanyAyamAha- 
adhikArAdInAM niravakAshatvAchcha | bahuvAkyAnurodho.apyatraiveti || 6 || 
|| adhikArAdInAmiti || "tattejo.asR^ijata tadapo.asR^ijata | tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itamekaikAmakarodityAderasya prakaraNasya bhUtAdhikAratvAt.h, Adipadokttasya kArShNyaprAchuryarUpapR^ithivIliN^gAdeH prasiddhAnne niravakAshatvAchcha "tA annamasR^ijanta' ityatrAnnashabdena pR^ithivyevochyata ityarthaH | nanu, pUrvapakShe bahuvAkyAnuvartitvasyokttatvAdanirNaya ityata Aha- bahuvAkyeti || atra siddhAnte | eveti vadatA pUrvapakShe bahuvAkyAnuvartitvasyAsiddhirukttA bhavati, "adbhayo vAnnamuchyate' ityAdAvannashabdasya pR^ithivIparatvAt.h "tadeva bhUyiShThamannaM bhavati' "annamashitam.h' ityAdau pArthivArthatvAt.h | evaMchAnnashabdasya pR^ithivyAmapi shakttimattvenAnnashruteH pR^ithivIparatvena shrutivirodhAbhAvAdapAM pR^ithivIkAraNatvasiddheryukttaM viShNorvastvantaradvArA jagatkAraNatvamiti 
bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "shabdAntara' iti "Apashcha pR^ithivI chAnnam.h' ityAdipR^ithivIshabdopetashrutyantaraparashabdaprayogena, "tasmAdyatra kva cha' ityAdipR^ithivIshabdarahitashrutivyAvartanAtsUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha "Apashcha pR^ithivI chAnnam.h' ityabhidhAnarUpashrutiparAntarashabdena sUchitaH | chashabdasUchitastvadhikArarUpetyanenokttaH |) || 6 || OM tadabhidhyAnAdeva tu talliN^gAtsaH OM || ityatra, "yatprayantyabhisaMvishanti rudro mAvishAntakaH' iti shrutivigAnenAdhibhUtAdhidaivAni kiM bhagavatA lIyante, rudreNa veti sandehe, rudreNaiveti pUrvaH pakShaH, bhagavataiveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "lokadR^iShyayanusAritvam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyamarthAttatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati - 
nacha rudrAdInAM layakAritvAN^gIkAre, pituranyasyaiva mArakatvadR^iShyerlokadR^iShyayanusAritvamiti guNaH | lokapitR^ivairUpyAdviShNoryathAvAkyamaN^gIkAropapatteH | anyathA na viShNoranyevilayakR^inna viShNoranyo vimukttidaH ityAdishrutivirodhAt.h |
|| nacha rudrAdInAmiti || Adipadena yamAdInAM grahaNam.h || pituranyasyeti || viShNostu  jagadutpAdakatvena pitR^itvAditi bhAvaH || loketi || loke cha pituranyasyaiva mArakatvadarshanAdityarthaH | evaMcha lokadR^iShyayanusAritvAtsarjakaviShNoranyasyaiva rudrAdeH saMhartR^itve.aN^gIkArye, viShNoH saMhArakatvAdishruteraprAmANyAnna jagatkatarR^itvAdi tasya yukttamiti netyarthaH | taddhetutvena "vairUpyam.h' ithyukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti - loketi || viShNomarmatvAdidoSharAhityena lokapitR^ivilakShaNatvAt.h, "idaM sarvaM vilApayati' ,"sraShyA pAtA cha saMhartA sa eko harirIshvaraH' ityAdishrutismR^itivAkyamanatikramya viShNoreva saMhartR^itvAN^gIkAropapatterityarthaH | nanu, rudrAdInAmeva saMhartR^itvAN^gIkAre bAdhakAbhAvAtkimiti lokavailakShaNyaM viShNoH kalpanIyamityata Aha- anyatheti || muktterapi layavisheShatvAt.h "na viShNoranyo vimukttidaH' iti shrutisheShodAharaNam.h | yadvakShyati "vimukttilayayovirsheShAbhAvAchcha' iti | nanu, "rudro mAvishAntakaH' ityAdivAkyAnAM kA gatirityata Aha-
rudrasya tu kvachitsaMhAradvAratvenaiva tadvAkyAnAM sAvakAshatvAt.h || 7 || nacha lokAnusAritvam.h | kramAdutpadyate, kramAdvilIyate, krameNaivotpattirvilayashcha krameNaivAsyotpattivilayau ityAdilokAnusAribahuvAkyAnurodhashcha yathotpattilaye |  
|| rudrasya tviti || rudrAdInAM tvityarthaH | saMhAradvAratvamapi na sarvatreti kvachidityukttam.h | tatashcha viShNorlokapitR^ivairUpyAdyukttaM tasyaikasyaiva sR^iShyisaMhArAdikartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra, pUrvapakShanyAyaH "saH' ityupAdakatvena prakR^itaparamAtmaparAmarshakena, tasyasaMhArakatarR^itvoktayA sUchito bhavati | siddhAntanyAyashcha, evakArArthakatushabdenotpAdakasyaiva saMhartR^itvoktayA sUchitaH | athavA visheShArthakatushabdenokttaH |) || 7 || OM viparyayeNa tu kramo.atra upapadyate cha OM || ityatra "ata eva hIdaM parAtkramAdutpadyate kramAdvilIyate', "akSharAtparamAdeva sarvamutpadyate kramAt.h | vyutkramAdvilayashchaiva' iti shrutivigAnena, adhibhUtAdIni kimutpattikramAnusAreNa lIyante, vyutkrameNa veti sandehe, utpattikrameNaiva (layaH) iti pUrvaH pakShaH, vyutkrameNaiveti siddhAntaH | tatra "lokadR^iShyayanusAritvam.h' iti prAgukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha loketi || loke utpattikramAnusAreNaiva layasya prAyikatvAditi bhAvaH | nyAyaM prakArAntareNa vivR^iNoti- kramAdutpadyata iti || ata eva lokAnusArItyukttam.h | yathotpattikrameNaiva laye | evaMcha lokadR^iShyayanusArikramashrutivirodhena vyutkramashruteraprAmANyavat.h shrutyantarasyApyaprAmANyAnna viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti cha netyarthaH | taddhetutvena "vairUpyam.h' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM pUrvapakShyudAhR^itashruteH shrutyaiva sAvakAshatvaM vadanvivR^iNoti- 
dvividhaH krama uddiShyo vyutkramo.anukramastathA | sR^iShyAvanyo laye chAnya iti vedavido viduH | iti shruteH kramavAkyasya sAvakAshatvAdvairUpyaM bahuprakAratvaM kramasya || 8 ||
|| dvividha iti || atra "vairUpyam.h' ityanuvAdena "bahuprakAratvam.h' iti vyAkhyAtam.h | anekaprakAratvamityarthaH | anena, rUpashabdaH prakAravachanaH, dvi(vi)vidhaM anukramatvavyutkramatvAkhyaM, rUpaM yasyeti virUpam.h, tasya bhAvo vairUpyamiti nyAyo vivR^ito bhavati | adhibhUtAdi, utpattikramavaiparItyenaiva lIyate, nacha lokAnusAribahuvAkyavirodhaH, kramasya vyutkramAnukramabhedenAnekaprakAratvAt.h "kramAdvilIyate' iti vAkyasya vyutkramaparatvena sAvakAshatvAt.h | nacha, kramAnekatve mAnAbhAvaH, dvividhaH iti shruteH ityarthaH | kuto netyatastAvatpUrvapakShyudAhR^itashruteH sAvakAshatvaM pradarshayati -dvividha iti || vyutkramAnukramabhedena kramasya dvaividhyAt.h kramavAkyasya vyutkramaparatvena sAvakAshatvAt.h, yathotpattivilaye na bahuvAkyAnurodha ityarthaH | sAvakAshatvaprakArameva vyaJNjayannyAyamanUdya vivR^iNoti- vairUpyamiti || bahuprakAratvaM anekaprakAratvamityarthaH | evaMcha kramasya vyutkramAnukramabhedena vairUpyAdvayutkrameNa laye.api shrutiprAmANyopapatteryukttaM viShNorjagatkartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra 
pUrvapakShanyAyaH "upapadyate cha' ityanena niShedhyatayA sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha "upapadyate' ityanenaiva sUchito bhavati |) || 8 || OM antarA vij~nAnamanasI krameNa talliN^gAditi chennAvisheShAt.h OM || ityatra "akSharAtparamAdeva' iti shrutyA, "prANAnmano manasashcha vij~nAnaM, yachChedvAN^manasI prAj~nastadyachChejj~nAna Atmani' iti liN^gadarshanena cha, kimadhibhUtAdIni sarvANyutpattikramavaiparItyena lIyante, kAnichitkrameNApi veti sandehe, sarveShAM na vyutkrameNa layaH, kintu keShAM chitkramAtkeShAJNchidvayutkramAditi pUrvaH pakShaH, sarveShAM vyutkrameNaiva laya iti siddhAntaH | atra lokadR^iShyayanusAritvamiti prAgukttameva nyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati -
nacha keShAJNchitkramAllayaH keShAJNchidvayutkramAllaya ityaN^gIkAre lokadR^iShyayanusAradantarA vij~nAnamanasI vyutkramaH | sarvaM vA etatkramAdutpadyate vyutkramAllIyate iti shrutau sarvasyApi vyutkramAllayasaN^grahAt.h | talliN^gasya tu charAcharavyApAshrayavij~nAnAdiviShayatvenaiva sAvakAshatvAt.h || 9 || 
|| nacha keShAJNchiditi || lokadR^iShyayanusArAditi | loke pituH purataH putrasya, putrasya purataH piturmaraNadarshanAdityarthaH | vyutkramaH ityanena "antarA vij~nAnamAnasI krameNa' ityatra kramashabdo vyutkramapara ityukttaM bhavati | nanvetat.h sambhAvakamevokttaM, na nishchAyakamitichetsatyam.h, tathApi "prANAnmano manasashcha vij~nAnam.h' iti manastattvotpannasya vij~nAnatattvasya, "yachChedvAN^manasI prAj~nastadyachChajj~nAna Atmani' iti manastattvalayAnantarameva layoktayanyAnupapattivilayanishchaya iti | evaMcha lokadR^iShyayanusAriliN^gadarshanena viruddhAyAH shruteraprAmANyAnna viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti cha neti bhAvaH | taddhetutvena "sarvasaN^grahaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- sarvaM vA etaditi || nanUkttaliN^gabalAt.h "sarvaM vA' iti shrutigatasarvashabdasyArthasaN^kochaH kriyata ityata Aha- talliN^gasya tviti || tasya vij~nAnamanasoryathotpattivilayasAdhakasyetyarthaH | Adipadena manograhaNam.h | shrutidvayAnyathAnupapattirhi liN^gam.h | tatra, yadyapi "yachChedvAN^manasI prAj~naH' ityeva tattvalayakramaH, tathApi nAyamutpattikramaH | nacha "manasashcha vij~nAnaM' iti shrutivirodhaH, tasyAH charAcharaviShayakavR^ittirUpaj~nAnasya, manorUpendriyajanyatvapratipAdakatvenaiva sAvakAshatvAdityarthaH | evaMcha "sarvaM vA' iti shrutau, lIyamAnasya sarvasyApi saN^grahAdvayutkrameNaiva layasiddheH shrutiprAmANyAdyukttaM viShNorjagatkAraNatvamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "antarA vij~nAnamanasI krameNa' iti keShAJNchitkramAllayasya, keShAJNchidvayutkramAllayasyoktayA sUchitaH | anyathA "vij~nAnamanasoH krameNa' ityavakShyat.h | siddhAntanyAyashcha "avisheShAt.h' ityanena sUchitaH |) || 9 || OM nAtmA shrutenirtyatvAchcha tAbhyaH OM || ityatra, "nityo nityAnAM, antastamasi nilInaH' iti shrutivirodhena, paramAtmA lIyate, na veti sandehe, lIyata iti pUrvaH pakShaH, na lIyata iti siddhAntaH | tatra "jIvasAmyam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUvarkaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha chetanatvena sAmyAdviShNorapi dehalayaH | 
|| nacha chetanatveneti || sAmyAt.h jIveneti sheShaH | viShNorityatrApi sambadhyate | tathAcha "viShNurlayavAn.h' chetanatvAjjIvavat.h ityukttaM bhavati | svarUpalayasyAsambhavAddehetyukttam.h | (anena sautraH pratij~nAMsho "nAmnA dehato lIyate' iti vyAkhyAto bhavati |) nacha "asambhavastu sato.anupapatteH' ityatra, svAtantyahetutA paramAtmano.anutpatterukttatvAtkathaM laya iti vAchyam.h, svatantrasya lIlayA vigrahagrahaNaparityAgopapattyAdhikAshaN^kayaitadadhikaraNotthAnAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha chetanatvena jIvasAmyeneshvarasya layasiddheH, prabalalayashrutivirodhena nityatvashruteraprAmANyAt.h, na viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti cha netyarthaH | kuto netyataH, tatra sAkShAddhetupradasharnapUrvakaM, tatsAdhakatvena "sarvasaN^grahaH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
sarve vA ete chidAtmano brahmaMllayamanuprApya viShNorudare saMvishantIti tasyodare sarvasaN^grahaNAdishrutibhyo nityatvAvagamAttaddehasya | ashrutatvAchchAnyathA || 10 || nachAnAditvAjjIvasya parAdhInavisheShAprAptiH | 
|| sarve vA iti || brahman.h brahmaNi, chaturmukhe | sarvasaN^grahaNAditi || pralaye viShNorudare sarveShAmapi chidAtmanAM saN^gR^ihItatvapratipAdakashrutibhya ityarthaH | viShNudehasyAnityatve, pralaye sarvasya tadudarasthatvaM na syAdityarthaH | (anena "nityatvAchcha' iti sautro heturvyAkhyAtaH |) sAdhakAbhAvAnna dehalaya ityAha- ashrutatvAditi || anyathA layatvena, nilInashruterapi hitatvaparatvAt.h, chetanatvayuktteH shrutivirodhenAprAmANyAdityarthaH | evaMcha pralaye viShNorudare sarvasaN^grahaNAttaddehasya layAbhAvAdyukttaM viShNorjagatkAraNatvamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "shruteH' iti jIvAdvisheShoktayA sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha "nityatvAchcha tAbhyaH' ityanena sarvasaN^grahAdishrutibhyo nityatvAvagamAditi pratipAdayatA sUchitaH |) || 10 || OM j~no.ata eva OM || ityatra, "nityo nityAnAm.h' "sarva ete chidAtmAno vyuchcharanti' iti shrutivibhAgena jIvaH 
kimutpadyate naveti sandehe, notpadyata iti pUrvaH pakShaH, utpadyata iti siddhAntaH | tatra "anAditA' ityuktta pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nachAnAditvAditi || jIvasyeti pUrvottarAbhyAM sambadhyate | jIvasya svarUpotpattyabhAvasya siddhAntinApyaN^gIkR^itvAdvivAdaviShayapradarshanArthaM parAdhInavisheShAprAptirityukttam.h | nachAkAshAdau vyabhichAraH, tasya pakShasamatvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha jIvasyAnAditayotpattyasambhavAnna sarvakartR^itvaM viShNoryukttamiti cha neti bhAvaH | taddhetutvena "sarvasaN^grahaH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti -
idaM sarvamasR^ijateti sarvasmingR^ihItatvAt.h | parAdhInavisheShavattve.apyanAditvasyAvirodhAt.h || 11 || nacha sarvadehasparshaj~nAnAdrasAdInAM cha tatratatra parij~nAnAjjIvasyAnaNutvam.h | utkrAntigatyAdeH | 
|| idaM sarvamiti || gR^ihItatvAt.h, jIvasyeti sheShaH | nanvanAditvabalAtsarvashabdasaN^kocha ityata Aha- parAdhIna iti || evaMcha "idaM sarvamasR^ijata' iti sarvapadArthe sarvasmin.h jIvasyApi saN^grahAttasyotpattisiddheryukttaM viShNorjagatkartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | ( atra pUrvapakShanyAyo.anAditve.apyutpattiryujyata ityarthapratipAdakena "yuktteshcha' iti sUtreNa sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha "ata eva' ityanena sarvasaN^grAhakashruterityarthapratipAdakena sUchitaH |) || 11 || OM utkrAntigatyAgatInAM OM || ityatra, "vyAptA hyAtmanaH' "aNurhyeSha AtmA' iti shrutivigAnena, jIvaH kiM vyApto.aNurveti sandehe, vyApta iti pUrvaH pakShaH, aNuriti siddhAntaH | atra, "tatratatra parij~nAnam.h' ityukttapUvarpakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati - nacha sarvadeha iti || jIvasyeti pUrveNottaroNa cha sambadhyate | evaMcha tatratatra sarvadehe, jIvasya sparshaj~nAnAttatratatra rasAdIndriyAdhiShThAneShu rasAdInAM yugapatparij~nAnAchcha jIvasya anaNutvaM aNutvAbhAvaH | evaMcha "AtmA kArtsnyam.h' ityatra dehaparimANasya nirastatvAtparisheShasiddhaM vyAptatvamiti cha netyarthaH | taddhetutvena "gatyAdiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- utkrAntigatyAderiti || anenAnuvyAkhyAnagatagatishabda upalakShaNArthaM ityukttaM bhavati | nanu, utkrAntigatyAdihetoH (nirAkR^itamadhyamaparimANasya) jIvasyANutve, sarvadehAdau sparshAdij~nAnopapattiH kathamityata Aha-

Ishashaktayaiva bahurUpatvAdeH || 13 || nacha shrutyA jIveshvaraikyam.h | sarvamAnavirodhAt.h | shruteH sAdR^ishyaikyAdiAna sAvakAshatvAt.h | bahumAnavirodhe ekasya daurbalyAchcha |

|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNabhAvabodhe dvitIyAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 
shrutyAdiprasiddhaprabalayuktayupetashrutInAmadhyAtmaviShayANAM parasparavirodhaparihArArthamayaM pAdaH pravR^ittaH | etatpAdIyAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAH saN^graheNAnuvyAkhyAyAmukttAH "tatra spaShyArthavachChrutiH | visheShashrutivairUpyaM mAhAtmyaM vyakttasadguNaH | dR^iShyA yukttiH samAnatvaM kartR^ishakttirvimishritA | yukttayaH pUrvapakSheShu sunirNItAstu tAdR^ishAH | yukttayo nirNa(yAyai)yasyaiva svayaM bhagavatoditAH ||' iti | tatra, || OM tathA prANAH OM || ityatra, "prANA evedamagra AsuH, atha prANA evAnAdayaH' iti "etasmAjjAyate prANaH' iti shrutivigAnena, prANAH kimutpattimanto naveti sandehe, notpattimanta iti pUrvaH pakShaH, utpattimanta iti siddhAntaH | tatra, "spaShyArthavachChrutiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha prANAnAmutpattyaN^gIkAre prANA evAnAdayaH ityAdispaShyAtharvadvisheShashrutivirodhaH | Atmaivedamagra AsItsa prANamasR^ijata sa prANAn.h ityAdivachanAdanAditva eva spaShyArthavadvisheShashrutivirodhAt.h | 
|| nacha prANAnAmiti || svapakShasAdhakasyaiva parapakShadUShakatvamiti j~nApayituM virodhamukhenaiva nyAyo vivR^itaH | anyathA "spaShyArthavadvisheShashruteH prANAnAmanAditvam.h' ityavakShyat.h | yadvA, "spaShyArthavachChrutiH' ityatra "visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' ityato "vairUpya' padamanukaSharNIyamiti bhAvenaivaM nyAyavivaraNaM kR^itam.h | evamanyatrApi draShyavyam.h | spaShyArthavatI- anAditvarUpaspaShyArthapratipAdikA, visheShashrutiH "prANA eva' iti prANarUpArthavisheShamadhikR^itya pravR^ittA, tayA virodhaH prANAnAmutpattyaN^gIkAra ityarthaH | evaMcha spaShyArthavachChrutyA prANAnAmanAditve.aN^gIkArye, na savarkartR^itvaM viShNoryukttamiti neti bhAvaH | kuto netyatastaddhetutvena, "spaShyArthavachChrutiH' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvenApi vivR^iNoti- Atmaivedamiti || asyA api shruteH "Atmaiva' ityavadhAraNenAnyAnAditvaniShedhakatvena, "asR^ijata' iti spaShyamutpattipratipAdakatvena, "prANaM, prANAn.h' ityarthavisheShamadhikR^itya pravR^ittatvena cha spaShyAtharvadvisheShashrutitvaM draShyavyam.h | evakAreNa prANAnAditvashruteH sAvakAshatvena siddhAntAvirodhakatvamAha | ata eva "sAvakAshAyAH' iti vakShyati | nacha evaM sati shrutidvayasyApi sAmyAtkathaM nirNaya ityata Aha- 
idaM sarvamasR^ijateti sAmAnyavachanasyAdhikyaM siddhAnte | visheShamAtrashruteH sAvakAshAyA ubhayashruteH prAbalyAt.h || 1 || nacha nityaM mano.anAditvAditi visheShashrutivirodhaH |
|| idaM sarvamiti || shrutitvAvisheShAtkathamanayA nirNaya ityata Aha- visheSheti || visheShashrutimAtrAditi yojanA | sUkShmarUpAnAditvapratipAdakatvena sAvakAshAyAH ityarthaH | evaMcha sAmAnyashrutisAhityena prabalaspaShyArthavadvisheShashrutyA, prANotpattisiddheryukttamIshvarasya shrutisamanvayena jagatkartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShanyAyaH "gauNyasambhavAt.h' ityanena, anAditvashrutergatiM vadatA sUchitaH | siddhAntanyAyashcha "asambhavAt.h' ityanena, utpattishrutyasambhavAdityarthakena, "pratij~nAnuparodhAchcha' ityanena chokttaH |) || 1 || OM tatprAk.hshruteshcha OM || ityatra, "etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH' iti, "tatra nityaM mano.anAditvAt.h' iti shrutivirodhena manaH kimutpattimanna veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, utpattimadeveti siddhAntaH | tatra "visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' ityukttaM nyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratiShedhati- nacha nityamiti || anishchitasya hetutvena kathanAsambhavAt.h, hetutayAnAditvapratipAdakatvena "nityaM manaH' iti vishiShya manoviShayatvena chAsyAH shrutervisheShaviShayatvaM j~nAtavyam.h | vairUpyamityasyArtho virodha iti | "manasa utpattimattve' iti sheShaH | evaMcha visheShashrutervairUpyAnmanaso.anAditvena sarvakartR^itvaM viShNoryukttamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo.anAditvashrutigatipradarshakasmR^itisamuchchAyakachashabdena vipakShabAdhakatarkarUpaH sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvenApi vivR^iNoti- 
etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi cheti visheShashruteH || 2 || nacha vAgvAva nityeti visheShashrutivirodhaH manaso vA va vAgutpadyate vAcho vyAharaNamiti visheShashruteH || 3 || 
|| etasmAditi || asyAH pR^ithaN^manaso janmAbhidhAyakatvena visheShashrutitvaM draShyavyam.h | shruteH shrutivirodhAt.h | "mano.anAditvasyeti sheShaH | nachAnAditvashrutivirodhaH tasyAH sUkShmarUpAnAditvaparatvAt.h | evaMcha manasa utpattipratipAdakavisheShashrutivirodhAt.h, na mano.anAditvamiti yukttaM hareH sarvakartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "shruteH' 
ityanena vipakShabAdhakatarkarUpa ukttaH | )|| 2 || OM tatpUrvakatvAdvAchaH OM || ityatra "sarvendriyANi cha' iti "na hyeShotpadyata' iti cha shrutivigAnena vAgindriyamutpadyate na veti sandehe, vAgindriyaviShayatve tasya chAnAditvaparatve chAsyAM hi shrutiravatiShThata iti vAkyasheShAdvisheShashrutitvaM j~nAtavyam.h | vAkyapadena shrutigrahaNe, shrutyAshrayatvAsambhavAt.h | nahi shrutau visheShashrutivairUpyAdvAgindriyasyAnAditve.aN^gIkArye.ayukttamIshasya sarvakartR^itvamiti cha neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH nAnutpattiriti anutpattiM niShedhatA anutpattAvupanyasanIyaM kiJNchitpramANaM sUchitam.h, tachchAtra pratyakShamanumAnaM vA na sambhavatIti shrutireva sUchitA, tadvairUpyalakShaNavipakShabAdhakatarka iti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' shrutivirodhAt.h, vAganAditvasyeti sheShaH | na vAgindriyasyAnutpattimattvAt.h , "manaso vA va vAk.h' iti manojanyatvashrutivirodhAt.h | nachAtra vAkpadaM vyAharaNaparamiti vAchyam.h, "vAcho vyAharaNam.h' iti vyAharaNahetutvashravaNAt.h, tasya cha vAgindriyaliN^gatvAditi bhAvaH | vAgindriyasya shrautAnAditvAnAdishrutyAshrayatvavirodhaparihArastu, "vAgindriyasya nityatvaM shrutisannidhiyogyatA | utpattirmanaso yasmAnna nityatvaM kutashchana ||' iti vachanena j~nAtavyaH | evaM chodAhR^itavachanasAhityena prabalavisheShashrutyA vAgindriyasyotpattisiddheryukttaM
