tatra, "visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' ityukttameva pUrvapakShasambandhitayA vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha dasheme puruShe prANAH AtmaikAdashaH' "sapta prANAH prabhavanti tasmAd.h' iti saN^khayAvisheShashrutyoreva parasparaM virodhaH | 
|| nacha dasheti || saN^khayAvisheShaH prANagatadashatvasaptatvarUpaH | tathAcha, dashatvasaptatvarUpavisheShapratipAdakashrutyoH parasparavairUpyeNAprAmANyAnna shrutyeshvarasya jagatkartR^itvasiddhiriti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH shrutigatipradarshakasmR^itisamuchchAyakachashabdena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvenApi vivR^iNoti- 
guhAshayayAM nihitAH saptasapteti saptabhAvasya buddhIndriyaviShayatvena visheShitatvAtsaN^khayAshrutyorviShayavailakShaNyAt.h || 4 || 
|| guhAshayAmiti || na saN^khayAshrutyoH parasparavirodhenAprAmANyam.h, dashatvashruteH paJNchakarmendriyapaJNchaj~nAnendriyaparatvam.h, saptatvashrutermanobuddhisahitashrotrAdisaptaj~nAnendriyaparatvamiti viShayavailakShaNyAt.h | nacha "sapta prANAH' ityuktAnAM j~nAnendriyatvaM kuta iti vAchyam.h, guhA hR^idayaM, AshayaH sthAnaM, yasyA buddhestAmuddishya shrotrasparshanarasanaghrANamanobuddhirUpAH pratisharIraM saptasapta nihitAH iti shrutau saptabhAvasya saptasaN^khayAyAH buddhIndriyaviShayatvena j~nAnasAdhanendriyaniShThatvena visheShitatvAdityarthaH | anena, visheShashrutyoH saN^khayAvisheShashrutyoH, vairUpyAt.h vilakShaNaviShayopetatvAditi nyAyo vivR^ito bhavati | evaMcha ("guhAshayAmiti'vAkyasheSheNa) visheShashruti(tyoH vailakShaNyAt.h)vairUpyAnna shrutyoH parasparaM virodha iti saN^khayAvisheShAnirNaya iti, shrutiprAmANyopapatteryukttaM hareH sarvakartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "visheShitatvAt.h' ityanenokttaH |) || 4 || OM aNavashcha OM || ityatra, "divIva chakShurAtatam.h' iti, "aNubhiH pashyati' iti shrutivigAnena prANAH kiM vyAptA utA.aNava iti sandehe, vyAptA iti pUrvaH pakShaH, aNava eveti siddhAntaH | tatra "visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- r
nacha divIva chakShurAtatamiti vyAptyAkhyavisheShavAchakashrutivirodhaH aNUni vA indriyANi teShAM prakAsho vyAtataH iti tato.apyaNutvavAchakavisheShashrutivirodhAt.h || 5 || 
|| nacha divIveti || virodhaH, prANANutvasyeti sheShaH | nanvaNutve.api shrutisadbhAvAtkathaM nirNaya iti chet.h(na), viShNorvyAptatve dR^iShyAntatvena chakShurvyApterukttatvena, etachChruteH prAbalyAt.h | atisudR^iDhasyaiva dR^iShyAntatvenopapAdanAt.h | evaMcha visheShashrutivirodhAdaNutvAbhAvenANutvashruteraprAmANyAnna shrutisamanvayena viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti cha neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo vyAptatvasamuchchAyakachashabdena, kevalANutvAN^gIkAre visheShashrutivirodha iti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena 
"visheShashrutivairUpyam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvenApi vivR^iNoti- aNUniti || atra, "teShAM prakAsho vyAtataH' iti "divIva' iti shrutisiddhavyAptatvamaN^gIkR^ityANutvasyokttatvAt.h, tato.api "divIva' iti shrutito.api, asyA visheShashrutitvaM j~nAtavyam.h | virodhaH svarUpeNa chakShurAdiprANavyAptatvasyeti sheShaH | evaMcha visheShashrutivirodhAt.h prANAnAmaNutvasiddheyarukttaM shrutisamanvayena viShNorjagatkAraNatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "aNavashcha' ityanena kevalavyAptyaN^gIkAre aNutvashrutivirodha iti sUchanena sUchitaH|) || 5 || OM shreShThashcha OM || ityatra, "naiSha prANa udeti' iti, "Atmata eSha prANo jAyate' iti shrutivigAnena, mukhyaprANa utpattimAnna veti sandehe neti pUrvaH pakShaH, utpattimAneveti siddhAntaH | tatra "mAhAtmyam.h' ityukttanyAyaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena, vAyuprokttavachanamudAhR^itya sAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvan.h pratikShipati- 
nacha yatprAptiryatparityAga utpattirmaraNaM tathA | tasyotpattimR^itishchaiva kathaM prANasya yujyate | ityAdimAhAtmyavachanAnmukhyaprANasya notpattiriti vAchyam.h | mahattvAnmahatAM viShNuH kartA prANasya chaikarAT.h | kiM nAma na sR^ijedeSha yena shaktayedamAvR^itam.h | iti shrutestato.api mAhAtmyAdviShNoH || 6 || 
nacha yatprAptiriti || evaMcha sarvajanmAdihetutvarUpamAhAtmyarUpayukttisahitAnAditvashrutivirodhenotpattishruteraprAmANyAnna shrutisamanvayena viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti cha neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH shreShThapadaprayogena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "mAhAtmyam.h' ityukttameva nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvenApi shrutyudAhAraNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- mahattvAditi || prANakartR^itve sarvakatarR^itvarUpaM hetvantaramAha- kiM nAmeti || yena svashaktayedaM savarM jagat.h AvR^itaM vashIkR^itameva, eva viShNuH kiM nAma na sR^ijet.h? sarvaM sR^ijedevetyarthaH | tato.apItyanena siddhAntanyAyasya prAbalyamAha | evaMcha prANasya prANotpAdakatvarUpAtimAhAtmyavadviShNujAtatvopapatteryukttaM shrutisamanvayena harejargatkAraNatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "na vAyukriyA' iti sUtragena "mukhyaprANaH paramAchcha' iti smR^itisUchakena "upadeshAt.h' ityanena sUchitaH |) || 6 || OM chakShurAdivattu tatsahashiShyayAdibhyaH OM || ityatra "na prANaH kiJNchidAshritaH' "prANasyaitadvashe sarvaM prANaH paravashe sthitaH' iti shrutivigAnena mukhyaprANaH svatantraH parantro veti sandehe, svatantra eveti siddhAntaH | asminnapyadhikaraNe "mAhAtmyam.h' ityanenaiva pUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAvabhihitau | "yadAshrayAdasya cheShyA so.anyaM kathamupAshrayet.h' ityukttasarvacheShyakatvarUpamAhAtmyena pUrvapakShotthAnAt.h, sarvakartApi san.h prANaH paramAdhArataH sthitaH' paramatvarapUmAhAtmyenaiva siddhAntitatvAt.h | etadevAbhipretyokttaM tatvaprakAshikAyAm.h - "akhilajagachcheShyakatvamAhAtmyavattvena' iti, "nanu svAtante yukttiyukttashrutisadbhAvAnna shrutimAtreNa nirNaya ityata Aha- sarveti' iti(cha) atra vivaraNaM tu pUrvAdhikaraNasambandhivivaraNenaiva kR^itam.h | ata eva pUrvAdhikaraNe "ityAdimAhAtmyavachanAt.h' iti AdipadaprayogaH | pR^ithagavivaraNaM tu pramANamAtrabhedena sarvasAmyAditi j~nAtavyam.h | (atra "akaraNatvAchcha' ityanena akaraNatvAdimAhAtmyaM pUrvapakShanyAya ityukttaM bhavati |) || 7 || OM paJNchavR^ittirmanovadvayapadishyate OM || ityatra "sarve vA ete mukhyadAsAH' iti, "mukhyasyaiva svarUpANi' iti shrutivigAnena prANAdayaH paJNcha kiM mukhyaprANasya dAsAH, uta svarUpANIti sandehe, dAsA eveti vA, svarUpANyeveti vA anyatarapakShaniyama eveti pUrvaH pakShaH, ubhayarUpA iti siddhAntaH | tatra, "vyakttasadguNAH' ityukttanyAyaM dvitIyapUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha prANAdipaJNchakasya vyakttasadguNatvAnmukhyaprANavR^ittitvameva | 
|| nacha prANAdipaJNchakasyeti || prANo.apAno vyAna udAnaH samana iti prANAdipaJNchakasya, "pAyUpasthe apAnaM chakShuHshrotre mukhanAsikAbhyAM prANaH svayaM pratiShThate | madhye tu samAna eShahyetaddhrutamannaM samaM nayati tasmAdetAH saptarchiSho bhavati nADIsahasrANyAsu vyAnashcharatyathaikayordhva udAnaH puNyena puNyaM lokaM nayati pApena pApaM pR^ithivyA yA devatA saiShA puruShasyApAnamavaShyabhya' ityAdivyakttasadguNatvAnmukhyaprANasya vR^ittimattvameva svarUpatvameva, natu dAsatvamityarthaH | dAsAnAmapi vyakttasadguNatve mukhyaprANasAmyena dAsatvameva na syAt.h | evaMcha vyakttasadguNebhyaH prANAdipaJNchakasya mukhyaprANasvarUpatve.aN^gIkArye dAsatvashruteraprAmANyAnna shrutisamanvayena viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM yukttamiti cha neti bhAvaH | taddhetutvena "vyakttasadguNAH' ityukttatvena nyAyaM siddhAntasambandhitvena shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
asheShaguNapUrNAni mukhyarUpANi paJNcha cha | taddAsAH paJNcha chAnye.api prANAdyAH sadguNairyutAH | iti shrutermukhyaprANasya tato.api vyakttasadguNatvAt.h || 8 || na chANutve prANasya mahAnvai mukhyaprANo yena vyAptaM charAcharam.h | iti dR^iShyAyukttiH | 
asheSheti || guNapUrNAni iti dAsApekShayA mukhyaprANasvarUpeShu guNAnAmAdhikyamAha- ata eva "dAsAH' sadguNairyutA' ityevokttam.h | mukhyaprANasya prANAdisvarUpasya, tato.api dAsebhyo.api vyakttasadguNatvAdityarthaH | tatashcha dAsAnAM vyakttasadguratve.api na 
mukhyaprANasAmyApattiH | evaMcha dAsebhyo.api svarUpANAmadhikavyakttasadguNatvenAdhikyopapatterdAsatvasvarUpatvasambhavAchChrutiprAmANyopapatteryukttaM shrutisamanvayena viShNorjagatkartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (imau cha nyAyau "vyapadishyate' ityanena "asheShaguNapUrNAni' iti shrutau asheShavyakttasadguNarUpatvena, vyakttasadguNarUpapaJNchadAsakatvena vyapadishyata ityukttaiH sUchitau |) || 8 || OM aNushcha OM || ityatra, "prANa evAdhastAt.h' iti, "aNunaitatsR^ijyate' ityAdishrutivigAnena mukhyaprANo vyApto na veti sandehe, vyApta eva mukhyaprANa iti pUrvaH pakShaH, aNureveti siddhAntaH | tatra "dR^iShyAyukttiH' ityukttatarkarUpapanyAyaM ApAdakapradarshanapUrvakaM pUrvapakShasambandhitvena vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- || nachANutva iti || mahAn.h vai vyApto vA iti pratij~nA | yena mukhyaprANena, charAcharaM sarvaM jagadvayAptamiti hetuH | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | "saptaskandhagato lokAnyo bibharti mahAbalaH' iti harivaMshavachanamapi grAhyam.h | tatashcha ityAdirUpapramANena dR^iShyasya nishchitasya sakalajagadvayApakasya, ayukttiH ayogaH, prANANutva ityarthaH | evaMcha dR^iShyAyuktayA mukhyasya vyAptisiddheraNutvashruteraprAmANyAnna shrutisamanvayena viShNorjagatkartR^itvaM yukttamiti cha neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH kevalANutvAN^gIkAre, "mahAnvai mukhyaprANaH' iti dR^iShyasya shrutyukttasya vyApakatvasyAyukttiH syAdityasmAnmahAttvasamuchchAyakashabdena sUchitaH |)  taddhetutvena "dR^iShyAyukttiH' ityukttatarkaparanyAyamApAdanapradarshanapUrvakaM siddhAntasambandhitvenApi vivR^iNoti- 
aNurvai mukhyaprANo ya utkrAmati nADIbhiH' itidR^iShyAyukttiranaNutve prANasya || 9 ||

|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNabhAvabodhe, shrIraghUttamayatikR^ite dvitIyAdhyAyasya chaturthaH pAdaH ||

OM tyAtmakatvAttu bhUyastvAt.h OM || ityatra "bhUtapariShvaktto raMhati' iti sAdhAraNavachanasyobhayathApyupapattyA, maraNe sarvabhUtAni kiM jIvaM pariShvajya gachChati, uta neti sandehe, na sarvANIti pUrvaH pakShaHSha, sarvANIti siddhAntaH | tatrA.anyathAnAmetyukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- iti tu paJNchamyAmiti || udAhR^itashrutau "bhUtAni' ityanuktavA, "ApaH' ityeva vachane apAmapi bhUtatvAtpUrvapakShasAdhakatvaM na syAdityataH sAmAnyanAmA.anuktavetyukttam.h | sAmAnyA(nAmA)pekShayA visheSha(nAmano)syA.anyathAtvA(tta)dvayAkhyAnArthaM visheShanAmetyukttam.h | apAmevetyevakArasAmarthyena na sarvabhUtAnAM jIvena sahagamanamiti sAdhyasiddhiH | evaMcha shrutau "ApaH' ityanyathAnAmoktteH samastabhUtapariShvaN^gA.abhAvAdekasya cha sharIrA.anArambhakatvAnmaraNa eva mokShasiddhervyarthaM vairAgyAdIti na vAchyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "bhUyastvAt.h' ityanena ap.hshabdaprayogagatiM vadatA sUchitaH | sAmAnyanAmA.apekShayA visheShanAmno.anyathAtvAt.h |) taddhetutvena "arthatobhava'

prANagaterupapattita ukttatvAt.h || 3 || nacha agniM vAgapyetItyAdyanyathoktteH prANAnAM cha na sahagatiH dvirUpatvAtprANAnAm.h || 4 || 
|| prANagateriti || prANagaterupapattita iti sAmAnAdhikaraNyam.h | "anuktteH' iti pUrvapakShadUShaNAya ukttatvAdityukttam.h, vastutaH siddhatvAdityatharH | ayaM bhAvaH | asti tAvadbhUtAnAmindriyairavinAbhAvaH, "yatra vA va bhUtAni tatra karaNAni' iti shruteH | ato vyApakaprANagatestadvayApyabhUtAnAM chAsti jIvena sahagatiH | tathAcha prayogaH- bhUtAni jIvena sahagamanavanti, tatsahagantR^iprANAvinAbhUtatvAt.h, yadyena saha yatrAvinAbhUtaM, tattena saha gachChati, yathA rAj~nA sahagantR^imAtyAvinAbhUtabhR^ityaH iti | tathAchopapattito bhUtagatisiddheH prAgukttaM yukttamiti | (ayaM cha nyAyo.avinAbhAvasUchakachashabdashiraskena "prANagateshcha' ityanenokttaH |) || 3 || OM agnyAdigatishruteriti chenna bhAkttatvAt.h  OM || ityatra, nirNAyakapramANAbhAvena, maraNe prANA jIvena saha gachChanti na veti sandehe neti pUrvaH pakShaH, gachChantIti siddhAntaH | tatra "anyathokttiH' ityukttanyAyaM sAdhyapradarshanapUvarMka vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- || nachAgnimiti || Adipadena "vAtaM prANashchakShurAdityaM manashchandramasaM dishaH shrotram.h' iti shrutisheShagrahaNam.h | jIvena sahAgatyuktayapekShayA vAgAdInAmagnyAdigatyuktteranyathAtvam.h | tatashcha prANAvinAbhUtabhUtAnAmapi jIvena sahagatiriti chashabdaH | evaMcha prANagateranyathoktteH prANAnAM jIvena sahagatyabhAvAttadvayAptabhUtAnAmapi sahagatyabhAvAnmaraNameva mokSha iti vairAgyAdivaiyarthyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo.agnyAdigatishruteH' ityanenokttaH |) taddhetutvena "dvirUpatvam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- dvirUpatvAditi || "puruShasya mR^itau brahmanprANA bhAgata eva tu | adhidaivaM prApanuvanti' iti pramANabalAtprANAnAM bhAgenAgnyAdInprati gatervidyamAnatvena tatrAsyeti shrutestadviShayatvAdityarthaH | evaMcha prANAnAM dvirUpatvAdekena rUpeNa jIvena sahagatisadbhAvAttadvayAptabhUtAnApyasti jIvena sahagatiriti na vairAgyAdivaiyarthyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "bhAkttatvAt.h' ityanenokttaH |) || 4 || OM prathame.ashravaNAditi chenna tA eva hyupapatteH OM || ityatra, maraNe sati jIvena sahagatimatprANAnAmanevaMvidhAnAM cha vastunAM darshanena, bhUtAni jIvena saha gachChanti na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, gachChantIti siddhAntaH | tatra avisheShetyukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha prathamato bhUtAni juvhatIti visheShAnuktterbhUtAnAmasahagatiH bhUtAni jahvatItyupakramAdapi iti tu paJNchamyAmAhutAvApaH puruShavachaso bhavantItyupasaMhArasyAdhikyAt.h tadanusAreNopakramokttashraddhAshabdasyApi tA evArtha ityApatteH | 
|| nacha prathamata iti || sUtre prathame iti atra prathamataH iti prathamAgnau upakrame iti chobhayArthakaM tantreNopAttam.h | visheShAnuktterityanena avisheShetyetat.h, visheShoktayabhAva iti vivR^itaM bhavati | yadi bhUtAnAM maraNakAle jIvena sahagatiH syAt.h, tarhi tasminnetasminnagnau devAH shraddhAM juhvati ityupakramavAkye, dvayAkhyaprathamAgnau shraddhayeShyavata utkrAntasya "shraddhAM juhvati' iti shraddhAsAhityena homashravaNavat.h, "bhUtAni juhvati' iti bhUtasAhityena homashravaNaM syAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha ("shraddhAM juhvati' itivadbhUtAni juhvatIti visheShoktayabhAvAt.h |) avisheShAdbhUtAnAM sahagatyAbhAvena maraNasyaiva mokShatvAdvayarthaM vairAgyAditi neti 
bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "prathame.ashravaNAt.h' ityanenopakrame "bhUtAni juhvati' iti visheShAktayabhAvAdityukttaH | ) taddhetutvena "Adhikyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM tatsAdhyatvena "tA eva hyupapatteH' iti sautrasiddhAntAMshArthapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- bhUtAnIti || atra "shraddhAm.h' iti vakttavye "bhUtAni' ityukttiH, "kimu "shraddhAM juhvati' ityupakramAt.h' iti kaimutyadyotanArthA | ata eva apipadaM, anyathA tadvayarthaM syAt.h | yadvA, bhUtAnAM sahagatau "bhUtAni juhvati' ityupakramaH syAditi yadukttaM tanna, "bhUtAni juhvati' ityupakramAdapi "iti tu paJNchamyAmAhutAvApaH' ityupasaMhArasyaivAdhikyAditi | tatashchaivamupakramAbhAve.api prabalopasaMhArabalAdbhUtAnAM sahagatiH siddhayatIti bhAvaH | (AdhikyAditi || ekaprakaraNe prathamenArthe dhIsthe, charamasya tadviShayasya prathamasthAchArasya, virodhenApyavaiyarthyAyAvashyakalpanIyakramavyAkhyAnasya prAbalyAdityarthaH | anena sautrahishabdAbhiprAya uktto bhavati | ) tA evetyevakAreNa sautreNAnUdite apAM, prastutatvaM shraddhAshabdArthatvasyAvashyakatvaM  chAha, natu shraddhAshabdasya, tadvayatirikttArthAntaravyAvR^ittim.h, shraddhAshabdenAjahallakShaNayA shraddhayAdbhishcha vishiShyasya jIvasya vivakShitatvAt.h | nanUpasaMhArasya vyAkhyAnatvena prAbalye.api kutastadanusAreNAtropakramokttashraddhAshabdasyArthakatvopapattirityataH "upapatteH' iti sUtrAMshAbhiprAyamAha-
upakramavirodhenopasaMhArAnupapatteH | upakramaprAmANyAtharmevopasaMhAritvamaN^gIkAryam.h | vyAkhyAnasya pashchAttanatvaniyamAt.h |
|| upakramavirodheneti || upasaMhArAnusAreNopakramArthakalpana eva prabalopasaMhAropapatteH, anyathA tadanupapatteriti bhAvaH | yadvA, durbalopakramavirodhena prabalopasaMhArasyArthAntarakalpanasyAnupapatteriti vyAkhyeyam.h | yadyupakramagatashraddhAshabdasya tanmAtrArthatvaM, tarhyapAmaprAptatvena "ApaH, puruShavachaso bhavanti' iti apAmanuvAdo na syAt.h | aprAptAnuvAdasyAsambhavena viruddhatvAt.h | nacha "parjanyo vA va gautamAgniH' ityAdivAkyAnAM madhyemAgarprAptasomAdiviShayatvAt.h "ApaH puruShavachaso bhavanti' ityupasaMhArasya madhyemArgaM prAptAbviShayakatvenAgamanamAtraviShayakatvaM vAchyam.h, "bhUtAni tyajati' ityanuktavA "somo rAjA sambhavati' ityAdivat.h, "Apo bhavanti' ityanuktavA "ApaH puruShavachaso bhavanti' ityanuvAdAditi | nanu tathApi, upasaMhArAnusAritvamupakramasya kuta ityata Aha- 
upakramaprAmANyArthamiti || evashabdenAN^gIkArasyAvashyakatvamAha | tathA chopasaMhArasyopakramavyAkhyAnarUpatvena prAbalyAdupakramaprAmANyopapattyarthamevopasaMhArAnusAritvamavashyamaN^gIkartavyam.h | vyAkhyAnAnanusArivyAkhyeyasya tadarthe prAmANyAdarshanAdityarthaH | anena "upapatteH' ityetadupakramaprAmANyopapatteriti prakArAntareNa vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | nanvavaiyarthyAnyathAnupapattyA kalpyamAnaM vyAkhyAnatvaparasyopasaMhArasyaiva nopakramasyetyatra ko visheShaheturityata Aha- vyAkhyAnasyeti || nopakramasya vyAkhyAnarUpatvaM kalpyam.h, tasya pashchAttanatvaniyamAt.h- tadvayAkhyAnaM tatpashchAttanamiti vyApteH | ataH parisheShAdusaMhArasyaiva pashchAttanasya vyAkhyAnarUpatvaM kalpyamiti bhAvaH | nanu "atha kasmAt.h' ityAdau vyAkhyAnasya pashchAttanatve.api "vAnAtsUterdevanAdvAsudevaH' ityAdau vyAkhyAnasya pUrvatanatvasyApi darshanena vyabhichArAtkathaM vyAkhyAnasya pashchAttanatvaniyama iti chenna, yato.atra pashchAttanatvaM nAma pashchAtpATho na vivakShitaH, kiM tu pashchAdupasthitam.h | loke vyAkhyeyopasthitiM vinA tadvayAkhyAne pravR^itterevAdarshanAdasambhavAchcha | tathAcha lokAnusAreNa vyAkhyeyavyAkhyAnayostadbhAvopapattaye pUvaropasthitatvaniyamasyAvashyakatve, "pAThakramAdarthakramo balIyAn.h' iti nyAyena vAnAtsUterityatrApi vyAkhyAnasyaiva pashchAdupasthitatvamaN^gIkAryam.h | upodghAtaprakriyayA pUrvapAThopapatteH | nanu "vAnAtsUteH' ityAdau pashchAtpaThitasyApi vyAkhyeyasya vAsudevAdipadasya pUrvamupasthitivat.h, pashchAtpaThitasyApyupasaMhArasya pUrvamupasthitisambhavena vyAkhyAnatvaprayojakapashchAdupasthitatvalakShaNapashchAttanatvamupasaMhArasyAsiddhamiti chenna, "vAnAsUteH' iti pUrvakAyasya pashchAtpaThitavAsudevapadavyAkhyAnatvavat.h upakramasyopasaMhAravyAkhyAnarUpatvasyAklR^iptatvena pAThakramApavAdakAbhAvAnniyatasvAdhyAyadashAyAM pAThakramAnusAreNa jAtayorupakramopasaMhAraviShayakopasthityoH pUrvatanatvapashchAttanatvaniyamasyaiva upasthitavirodhakatvarUpopasaJNjAtavirodhitvasambhavAt.h | upasthitishcha pauruSheyavAkye praNetuH puruShasya, vedetvIshvarasya | tatreshvarAbhiprAyapraveshena tasyeshvaravAkyatvAt.h | yathokttaM tatvanirNayaTIkAyAM - "puruShAbhiprAyapraveshe.api' iti | karmanirNayaTIkAyAM cha - "vedo.apauruSheya ityasmAkaM, pareShAM cha yadyapi samam.h  tathApIshvaravAkyatvaM samastasyApi vedasya vayamaN^gIkurmo, na pare iti | nanu tathApyupakrama evopasaMhArApekShayA prabala ityaN^gIkartavyam.h | upakramAbhAve, upasaMhArasvarUpaniShpatterevAbhAvena upasaMhArasyopajIvakatvAt.h | yena vinA hi yasyAnutthApanaM, tattasyopajIvyam.h | nahyanupakrAntasyopasaMhAro.astItyAshaN^kaya pariharati- 
upakramAnusAritvaniyame.apyupasaMhArasyopasaMhAreNaivopakramArtho j~nAyate || 5 || nacha visheShAshravaNaniyama eva balavAn.h 
sthAnAntarashravaNasyApyetadanurUpatvAt.h | 
|| upakrameti || anusAritvaM sApekShatvam.h | "api' padena "yena vinA yasyAnutthAnaM tattasyopajIvyam.h' ityasya bhramabodhAdau vyabhichAraM sUchayati | tathAcha yadyapi svarUpeNopasaMhArArasyopakramasApekShatvaniyamaH , tathApi "nadaM va odatInAm.h' ityAdimantrasya, "tA nadena viharati' ityAdinishchitaprAmANyanirNayAdAvupakrama evopasaMhArasApekSha ityarthapratItyA(dau)upasaMhArasyaiva prAbalyamityaN^gIkAryamiti bhAvaH | etenaivopakramopasaMhArayoranupasaJNjAtavirodhitvAbhyAM prAbalyadaurbalye ityapi parAstam.h | bhramabodhAdau vyabhichArAditi ityupasaMhAropapatteriti sUchitaH | anyathA "tA eva' ityavadhAraNAnupapattiH |) || 5 || OM ashrutatvAditi chenneShyAdikAriNAM pratIteH' OM || ityatra pUrvavat.h ubhayavidhavastudarshanena maraNe bhUtAni jIvena saha gachChanti na veti sandehe, na gachChantIti pUrvaH pakShaH, gachChantIti siddhAntaH | tatra "avisheShaH' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha visheShAshravaNeti || yatrAsya puruShasya mR^itasya vAgagnimapyeti prANAnAmagnyAdIn.h prati gatipratipAdakapratyakShashrutivat.h bhUtAnAM jIvena saha gatipratipAdakapratyakShashrutyabhAvaniyama evetyarthaH | balavAniti "iti tu paJNchamyAmAhutAvApaH' iti abgatishravaNarUpabhUtagatigocharArthikashravaNAdvayApakagatau vyApyagatirAvashyakIti nyAyena bhUtavyApakaprANagatishravaNarUpabhUtagatigocharArthikashravaNAdapIti bhAvaH | ata eva "tyAtmakatvAt.h' "prANagateshcha' ityAdinA nirNItatvAnnaivaM saMshayAdyavakAsha iti na vAchyam.h, tadupamardenAbhyadhikAshaN^kAyAH pratyavasthAnam.h | evaMcha visheShAshravaNarUpAvisheShAnna bhUtAnAM sahagatiriti vairAgyAdivaiyathyarmiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "ashrutatvAt.h' ityanena visheShashravaNAbhAva ityukttaH |) taddhetutvena "anurUpatA' iti siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- sthAnAntareti | "athainaM yajamAnaM kiM na jahAti bhUtAnyeva bhUtaireva gachChati' iti sthAnAntare jIvena saha bhUtAnAM gatishravaNasyApi, etadanurUpatvAdAthirkashravaNAnukUlatvAt.h, ArthikashravaNamevAshravaNaniyamApekShayA prabalamityarthaH | natvArthikashravaNasya neShyAdikAriNAmiti sthAnAntarashravaNAnukUlyakathanaM vyartham.h | ArthikashravaNAsyaivAshravaNavAchakatvopapatteH | nacha ArthikashravaNasya bAdhakatvopayogiprAbalyAya saMvAditvena tatkalpanamiti vAchyam.h | saMvAdakapramANAbhAve.api prANagatirUpayukttervyAptipakShadharmatayoH shrutisiddhatvenApAM gaterupasaMhArarUpapramANasiddhatvenArthikasya prAbalyopapattau tadarthaM tasyAvakttavyatvAdityata Aha- 
ArthikashravaNamapyanukttiM bAdhata eva kimu sthAnAntaragataM spaShyashravaNamiti | kaimutyArthameva neShyAdikAriNAM pratIteriti parihArAntaramukttam.h || 6 ||
|| ArthikashravaNamiti || anukttiM bAdhata eveti yuktterapi vyAptiliN^gagrAhakaprAmANyenaiva bhavitavyam.h | tachcha bhUtAnAM prANavyAptatvena, prANAnAM jIvena sahagatau shrutirUpam.h, apAM sarvabhUtAtmakatvena jIvena sahagatau shrutyupasaMhArarUpamastIti, ArthikashravaNasyApi visheShashravaNavadashravaNabAdhakatvamityarthaH |) evaMcha rathAntarashravaNasyArthikashravaNAnurUpatvAt.h, bhUtAnAM sahagatirupapannaiveti na vairAgyAdi vaiyarthyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "iShyAdikAriNAM pratIteH' ityanena "athainaM yajamAnamiti sthAnAntarashravaNasyApItyetadanurUpatvamityukttaH |) || 6 || OM bhAkttaM vAnAtmavittvAttathA hi darshayati OM || ityatra, phalArthamavashyAnuShTheyAnanuShTheyasAdhadarshanAdvairAgyasAdhanaM kiM mumukShuNAvashyakamunuShTheyaM naveti sandehe, nAvashyamanuShTheyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, avashyamanuShTheyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra visheSha ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvaMka vivR^iNvanpratikShipati - 
nacha apAmasomamR^itA abhUmeti visheShata eva mokShaphalasyApyuktteH karmaiva mokShasAdhanamiti na mantavyam.h |
|| nacha apAmasometi || apAmiti shrutau "amR^itA abhUma' iti visheShAkAreNaiva mokSharUpaphalasya sAkShAtkarmasAdhyatoktteH svargAderiva mokShasyApi j~nAnadvAramantareNa karmaiva sAdhanamityarthaH | evaMcha "apAmasomam.h' iti vachanavisheShAtkarmaiva mokShasAdhanamiti vairAgyAdivaiyarthyamiti na mantavyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "bhAkttam.h' ityanena "apAm.h' iti shrutergatikathanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "yogyatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
nAnyaH panthA ayanAya vidyate sa ya AtmAnameva lokamupAste yAvadindro yAvanmanurityAdi shrutibalAdamR^itashabdasya yathAyogyamevArthakalpanoktteH || 7 || 
|| nAnyaH panthA iti || yathAyogyamiti somayAgAdikarmaNaH kAmyasya bahukAlInatvaguNayogena svargAkhyagauNAmR^itatvasya 
kAmyatve.api, jij~nAsukR^itakarmaNo j~nAnadvArA pAramparyeNaiva mukhyAmR^itatvasya tadekadeshalakShaNayA, j~nAnikR^itasya tu lakShaNayAmR^itatvasAdhanena (j~nAnarUpAmR^itatvasya vA) Atmaj~nAnalabdhamokShe AnandAbhivR^iddhilakShaNAtishayarUpAmR^itatvasya (vA) shrutigatAmR^itashabdArthatvena yogyatvAttasyaivArthasya kalpanopapatteH | sa(rvathA)rvAtmanA na karmaNA sAkShAtsaMsAranivR^ittiH shrutyarthaH (ityarthaH|) kuto naivaM shrutyartha ityata ukttam.h - nAnyaH panthA ayanAya vidyata iti || amR^itashabdasya, AnandAbhivR^iddhirUpamuktayarthatve shrutimAha- sa ya iti || svargAkhyagauNamuktayarthatve cha tAmAha- yAvadindra iti || Adipadena pAramparyeNa mokShasAdhanIbhUtaj~nAnasAdhanatve cha "karmaNA j~nAnamAtanoti' iti draShyavyA | atra sautrabhAkttashabdena prathamaH pakShaH, vAshabdAtpakSha(dvayaM)trayaM j~nApitamiti j~nAtavyam.h | yadyapi bhAShyataTTIkayoH pakShadvayameva vAshabdArthatvenokttam.h, tathApi karmanirNayaTIkAyAM "amR^itashabdasya tatsAdhanaj~nAnalakShaNayA' iti pakShAntaramapyetatsUtrArthatayokttamiti | evaMcha shrutyarthatayAnekeShAM yogyatayA vairAgyAdyanuShThAnamantareNa mokShAsiddherna vairAgyAdivaiyarthyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "bhAkttaM vA' ityanena shruteryathAyogyamarthavarNanena sUchitaH |) || 7 || OM kR^itAtyaye.anushayavAndR^iShyasmR^itibhyAm.h OM || ityatra, pUrvAdhikaraNokttanyAyatadanapekShaphalaniShpattidarshanAbhyAM vairAgyAdikaM mumukShuNAvashyamanuShTheyaM na veti sandehe, nAnuShTheyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, avashyamanuShTheyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, "sahabhAva' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nachAnushayasya sahabhAvAtsvarga eva phaladatvam.h bhukttasheShAnushayavAnityAdivachanAdyathAyogyameva phaladAnopapatteH || 8 || nacha mArgasyApi sahabhAvAdyathAgatamevAgamanamiti niyamaH | 
|| nachAnushayasyeti || anushayasya, (bhukttakarmasheShasya) karmaNaH, svargaM gachChatA jIvena sahabhAvAt.h, svarge.akiJNchitphala(da)tvAN^gIkArAdevetyukttam.h | evaMcha karmaNaH sahabhAvena svarga eva phala(da)tvopapatteH, tatra karmAntaropAdAnAbhAvAt.h karmAbhAve cha tanmUlasaMsArochChedaH svayameva bhavatIti na mumukShuNAvashyamanuShTheyaM vairAgyAdIti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "kR^itAtyaye.anushayavAn.h' ityanena karmaNA sahabhAvAditi sUchitaH | sahabhAvA.abhAve, atyaye.anushayavattvaM cha na syAt.h |) taddhetutvena "yogyatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyameva vivR^iNoti- bhukttasheSheti || Adipadena "yataH sheSheNa' iti shrutigrahaNam.h | smR^iteH shrutyapekShayA vivakShitAsheShArthapratipAdakatvAtpratIkena nyAyaH "anushayavAn.h' ityanenaiva karmaNA yathAyogyameva phaladatvamiti sUchitaH | yadvA "dR^iShyasmR^itibhyAm.h' iti pramANe visheShoktayA sUchitaH |) || 8 || OM yathetamanevaM cha OM || ityatra, yathAgamanamanyathA cha gamanadarshanAtsarvaM gataH kiM gatiprakAreNAgachChatyanyathA veti sandehe, gatiprakAreNaiveti pUrvaH pakShaH, anyathA cheti siddhAntaH | tatra "sahabhAvaH' iti pUrvokttameva pUvarpakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha mArgasyeti || "saha' ityataH pUrvaM "mana(si)saH' iti sheShaH | siddhAntinA gamanasyobhayathApyaN^gIkArAt.h  evetyukttaM tasyaiva vivaraNaM niyamaH iti | nahi vij~nAtaM panthAnaM vihAyAvij~nAtena gamane prayojanamastItyarthaH | evaMcha gamana(mAgar)sya smR^itiviShayatayA manasi sahabhAvena, tenaiva gamanasambhave, svargaphalasyApi kleshAnuShaN^gAbhAvAdvairAgyAdivaiyarthyamiti neti bhAvaH | ayaM cha nyAyaH "yathetam.h' ityanena mArgasya saMskAraviShayatvena manasi sahabhAva iti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena pUrvokttameva "yogyatA' iti siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
vachanabalAdyathAyogyamevAgamanopapatteH || 9 || nacha iShyApUtare dattamityupAsata ityupashabde neShyAdibhirAchArasya sahapAThAchcharaNaphalaM punarAvR^ittiM karaNaphalatvena bhramAdvadantIti vAchyam.h | 
|| vachanabalAditi || "dhUmAdabhram.h' iti visheShavachanabalAdyogyaM mArgamanatikramyaivAgamanopapatterityarthaH | (nacha sahabhAvarUpayukttivirodhaH, Agamane jIvasyAsvAtanteNa tatsmaraNasyAgamanAnupayogitvenAprayojakatvAt.h | ata eva yathAyogyameveti niyamavyavachChedAyAvadhAraNam.h |) evaMcha mArgadvayasyApi yogyatayA svargAdAgamanasyAtikleshAnuShaN^gAnna vairAgyAdivaiyarthyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "yathetamanevaM cha' ityanena yathAyogyamevAgamanamiti sUchitaH |) || 9 || OM charaNAditi chenna tadupalakShaNArtheti kArShNAjiniH OM || ityatra, gatAgatanimittayorubhayorapi sahabhAvadarshanena yaj~nAdikaM gatAgatasAdhanaM na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, sAdhanamiti siddhAntaH | atrApi sahabhAva ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacheShyApUrteti || na gatAgataM yaj~nAdi karmaphalam.h, kintu charaNaphalameva, "ramaNIyacharaNAH, kapUyacharaNAH' iti shruteH | nacha tayorabhedaH, "achAra iti samprokttaH karmAN^gatvena shuddhidaH' iti smR^iteraN^gAN^gibhAvena bhedAt.h | nanu, "atha ya ime grAmA iShyApUrte dattamityupAsate te dhUmamabhisambhavanti' ityupakramya, "tasminyAvatsampAtamuShitvAyaitamevAdhvAnaM punarAvartante' iti shrutegartatAgatasya yaj~nAdiphalatvapratIterayukttaM 
charaNaphalatvakalpanamityata ukttam.h- charaNaphalamiti || punarAvR^ittimityekadeshotkIrtanaM, "gamanamapi' ityapi grAhyam.h | yadyapyanayA shrutyA gatAgatasya yaj~nAdiphalatvapratItijarAyate, tathApi sA bhrAntireva, gatAgatasya charaNaphalatvAdityarthaH | nanu kR^itaH, bhrAntinimittAbhAvAdityata ukttam.h- iShTAdibhirAchArasyeti || upalakShaNametat.h, svargeNa gatAgatasya sahapAThAdityapi draShyavyam.h | tathAcha iShyAdibhirAchArasya, svargeNa gatAgatasya cha sahokttireva bhrAntinimittamityarthaH | syAdetat.h, yadyatra iShyAdibhirAchArasya sahapATha eva bhavet.h, sa eva kutaH, tadvAchakapadAshravaNAdityata ukttam.h- iShyApUrteti || tathAcha "upa'shabdasya samIpavartivastuvAchakatvAdAchArasya cha yaj~nAdisamIpavartitvAt.h "upAsitaH' iti "upa'shabdena, iShyAdibhirAchAraH sahapaThita ityarthaH | nanvevamapi bAdhakAbhAvAtkuto bhrAntitvamiti chenna, charaNashruterviShayAntarAbhAvenAprAmANyasyaiva bAdhakatvAditi | evaM cheShyAdipadoditayajanAdirUpashabdokttacharaNasya sahabhAvAnimittAcharaNaphalameva gatAgatamiShyAdikaraNaphalamityutpannaj~nAnasya bhramatvAnneShyAdi gatAgatasAdhanaM, kiM tu apunarAvR^ittiphalasAdhanamiti na tadarthaM vairAgyAdi sampAdanIyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "charaNAn.h' ityananyathAsiddhahetuM vadatA "atha ya ime grAmAH' iti shrutau, karaNacharaNayoH sahapAThanimittakagatAgatasya karaNaphalatvapratItirbhrAntiriti bAdhakoddhAro.api sUchito bhavati iti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena pUrvokttameva "yogyatA' iti siddhAntanyAyaM hetupradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
nAnyaH panthA ityAdivachanAdevobhayarorapi charaNashabdenaivoktteyarogyatvAt.h || 10 || nacha bhayaphalakAmAdimishrabuddhitvAdiShyAdikAriNAM saMsAraH aniShyAdikAriNAM tadabhAvAnmukttiriti vAchyam.h | 
|| nAnyaH panthA iti || na charaNashrutyanyathAnupapattyA gatAgatasya yaj~nAdiphalatvapratItirbhrAntiriti kalpyam.h, tasyA anyathopapatteH | charaNashabdenaivAjahallakShaNayA mukhyavR^ittyA chobhayoH, karmAcharaNayorapyuktteH, pratipAdanasya, yogyatvAt.h, sambhavAdityarthaH | nanu, ubhayorapi kimarthaM karmaNa ityeva vakttavyamiti chenna, karmakartR^iNAM ramaNIyatvAdeshcharaNasApekShatvena charaNAgrahaNe tadalAbhAt.h | nanu, gatAgatasya charaNaphalatvameva kiM na syAt.h, bAdhakAbhAvAdityata ukttam.h- nAnya iti || evakAreNa shruterniravakAshatvamAha | Adipadena "iShyApUrtam.h manyamAnAH' "atha ye yaj~nena dAnena tapasA lokAJNjayanti te dhUmamabhisambhavanti' ityAdishrutiH, "traividyA mAm.h' ityAdismR^itishcha grAhyA | tathAcha "nAnyaH panthAH' ityAdi shrutyA karmaNaH punarAvR^ittishUnyaphalakatvasya niShiddhatvAt.h "traividyAH' ityAdismR^ityA tatphalakatvadarshanAchcha, "atha yaH' ityAdisamAkhyAnAchcha yukttaM charaNashrutivyAkhyAnamityarthaH | evaMcha gatAgatasya karmaphalatvAtkleshasAdhane, tasminsAdhye cha virakttena bhAvyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tadupalakShaNArthaH' ityanena "nAnyaH panthAH' iti bAdhakavashena karaNacharaNayoshcharaNashabdenoktteryogyatvAdityukttaH || 10 || OM aniShyAdikAriNAmapi cha shrutam.h OM || ityatra, iShyApUtyarAdivisheShoktayaj~nAnitvAbhyAM gatAgataM kimiShyAdikAriNAmevota sarvAj~nAninAmapIti sandehe, iShyAdikAriNAmeveti pUrvaH pakShaH, sarvAj~nAninAmiti siddhAntaH | tatra, vimishratetyukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratiShedhati- nacha bhayeti || bhayetyataH pUrvaM "pratyavAyaH' iti grAhyam.h | kAmAdIti Adipadena vidhipratiShedhabandhaparigrahaH | saMsAra iti "bibhyatpatati pAdapAt.h' iti nyAyAditi bhAvaH | mukttiriti svargamuktayatirikttaM phalAntaraM nAstIti pUrvapakShyabhiprAyaH | evaMcha vimishrabuddhitvAdiShyAdikariNAmeva gatAgatamiti niyamo neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "aniShyAdikAriNAmapi' ityanena pratyavAyabhayena phalakAmanayA yajanAdikarma kurvatAM samuchchayena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "balavattvam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
teShAM prabaladoShashruteH || 11 || nacha narakabhogasyAnityatvakathanAnnityanarakokttirviruddhA |
|| teShAmiti || prabaletyanena saMyamane tvanubhUyetyAdisUtrokttaduHkhAdidoShasaN^graho.api kR^itaH | (evaMcha bhayakAmanAdyabhAvavirodhaH | bibhyatA phalakAmashUnyenApyukttaviShayasya maraNahetutvAdarshanAt.h |) evaMcha balavaddoShashrutyAj~nAnAM sarveShAM gatAgatamastIti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH prathamasUtrArthachashabdena dvitIyatR^itIyasUtrAbhyAM cha doShabalavattvamityukttaH |) || 11 || OM apisapta OM || ityatra "avarohaH' iti pUrvoktayA, lokadR^iShyayA cha narakaM nityaduHkhapradamuta neti sandehe, punarAvR^ittipradameveti pUrvaH pakShaH, nityaduHkhapradamiti siddhAntaH | tatra "viruddhokttiH' ityukttapUvarpakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha narakabhogasyeti || anityatvakathanAt.h - "yAvadindrAshchaturdasha | chakAra narakaM shUnyam.h' ityAdAvityarthaH | evaMcha narakasyAnityatve pramite, tannityatvoktterviruddhatvena, nityanarakAdbhakavaddveShiNAmapyanityaM narakamiti na bhagavaddveShAdau, atishayena vairAgyAdyApAdyamiti pakSho neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo narakANAM nityatvAnityatvavibhAgakathenenAnityatvoktayA nityatvokttirviruddheti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "vibhAgaH' iti ukttasiddhAntanyAyaM smR^ityudAhAraNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
rauravo.atha mahAँshchaiva vahnirvaitaraNI tathA | kumbhIpAka iti prokttAnyanityanarakANi tu | tAmisrashchAndhatAmisro dvau nityau samprakIrtitAviti vibhAgAt.h || 12 || nacha sahasthAnAdIshasyApi narakaduHkhaprAptiH | svAtantAtkAraNAbhAvAt.h || 13 ||
|| raurava iti || vibhAgAt.h narakANAM nityatvAnityatvAbhyAmityarthaH | evaMcha narakANAM vibhAgAnna nityatvokttirviruddheti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "api saptaH' iti sUtreNaivokttaH |) || 12 || OM tatrApi cha tadvayApArAdavirodhaH OM || ityatra, duHkhayukttatadrahitajAgradAdidvividhAvasthAdarshanAnnarakaM kiM saduHkhaM, na veti saMshaye, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, saduHkhamiti siddhAntaH | tatra sahasthAnamityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha sahasthAnAditi || Ishasyeti vadatA "sarvaM ramayati' iti shrutibalena narake.api nArakijananiyamanArthaM Ishena sthAtavyamiti sahasthAnaM nAsiddhamiti sUchitaM bhavati | yadvA, "IshasyApIti' siddhAntyaniShyatvamAha | evaMcha narakasya saduHkhatve, IshasyApi saduHkhasahasthAnAt.h saduHkhatvaM syAditi, narakaM nirduHkhameveti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tatrApi' ityanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "kAraNAbhAvaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM hetupradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- svAtantAditi || asvatantre hyanapekShitAnyaj~nAnAdiduHkhakAraNAni sambhavanti, Ishvarasya svatantratvAtsarvaj~natvenAj~nAnAdiduHkhakAraNAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha duHkhakAraNAbhAvAdIshvarasya narake sahasthAneShvapi, na duHkhaprAptiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo duHkhAnubhavasamuchchAyakachashabdena sUchitaH |) || 13 || OM vidyAkarmaNoriti tu prakR^itatvAt.h OM || ityatra, laukikamArge svAtantyadarshanenAlaukikatvena cha, pitR^iyAnadevayAnau kiM bhUtaiH svAtanteNa gamyau, na veti sandehe, svAtanteNa gamyau, iti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "sahasthAnam.h' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha sAdhanena saha shrutestadvatphale.api jIvasya svAtantyam.h | avihitatvena kAraNAbhAvAt.h | 
|| nacha sAdhaneneti || "tadya itthaM vidurye cheme.araNye shraddhAtapa ityupAsate' "te.achirShamabhisambhavanti' "atha ya ime grAmA iShyApUrte dattamityupAsate te dhUmamabhisambhavanti' iti shrutau, vidyeShyAdisAdhanena saha, archirAdidhUmAdibhAvalakShaNa(sya)phalasya shravaNAt.h, tadvatsAdhana iva, phale.api svAtantyamaN^gIkAryam.h, sAdhane svAtantAbhAve tu, vairAgyAdisAdhanamapi notpAdayituM shakyaM syAditi tadvidhivaiyarthyaprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha (phalasyaiva sAdhayituM shakyatvAt.h) phalArthaM na vairAgyAdikamApAdyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "prakR^itatvAt.h' ityanena devayAnapitR^iyANavat.h vidyAkarmaNoH prakR^itatvAditi sUchitaH | ata eva bhAShye "tayorapi' ityapishabdaH |) taddhetutvena "kAraNAbhAvaH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- avihitatveneti || phalasye(tyarthaH)ti sheShaH | anena svAtantyavihitatvaM kAraNaM, tachcha vairAgyAdisAdhane brahmaNo nirvedamAyAdItyAdinA pramitaM vidhyAdishAstrA.avaiyarthyAya hi, tatreshvaraH svAtantyaM dadAtIti "kartA shAstrArthavattvAt.h' ityatrokttam.h | phale tu vihitatvAbhAvAt.h na sAdhanapratibandigrahaNaM yukttamityukttaM bhavati | nanu tarhi, "athaitayoH pathoH' iti shrutau "naikatareNa' iti kathaM mArgeNa gatiniShedhaH, nahi puruShaprayatnAviShayena(Na)gachChantIti prayogo yujyata ityata Aha- 
athaitayoH pathorityasya cha sAdhanArthatvAt.h || 14 || nacha duHkhasahasthAyitvAdandhetamasyapi sukham.h | IshasyApriyatvenaiva kAraNAbhAvAt.h || 15 || 
|| athaitayoriti || sAdhanArtatvAditi devayAnapitR^iyANarUpamArgadvayasAdhanatayA prakR^itavidyAkarmaviShayatvAdityarthaH | evaMcha vihitatvarUpakAraNAbhAvAtphale jIvasya svAtantAbhAvena tadarthaM vairAgyAdikamApAdyameveti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, tushabdena vidyAkarmaNovirhitatvarUpavisheShasyokttatvAdeva devayAnapitR^iyANayoH phalabhUtayorvihitatvarUpakAraNAbhAvasUchanena sUchitaH |) || 14 || OM na tR^itIye tathopalabdheH OM || ityatra, duHkhavataH sukhadarshanena, alaukikatvena (cha), andhantamaH sukhayukttaM na veti sandehe, sukhayukttameveti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | atrApi "sahasthAnam.h' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUvarkaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha duHkheti || (sukhasyeti sheShaH) duHkhasya sukhena sahAvasthAyitvAt.h vyAptatvAdityarthaH | tathAcha nAprayojakatA | nacha vakttavyaM savarsukhaduHkhayorapratyakShatvAdvayAptigrahaNAnupapattiriti, "yatra duHkhaM sukhaM tatrA' ityAgamena vyAptigrahaNopapattiriti bhAvaH | evaMcha duHkhasya sukhena sahAvasthAnAt.h tamaH prAptAnAmapi sukhasambhavAttatsAdhane bhagavaddveShAdau nAtishayena evairAgyamApAdyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tathopalabdheH' ityanena, tR^itIyatamovyatirikttanarakeShu sukhaduHkhayoH sahasthAnapratipAdakashrutigrAhakeNa sUchitaH | ) taddhetutvena "kAraNAbhAvaH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- Ishasyeti || kAraNetyataH pUrvaM IshechChArUpetyadhyahAryam.h | idamukttaM bhavati- vipratipannA na sukhavantaH, tathAtveneshvarAniShyatvAt.h, yadyatheshvarAniShyaM tattathA na bhavati, yathA shasho viShANitvena iti | hetvasiddhiparihArArtamukttam.h - 
apriyatvenaiveti || apriyatvahetoH atyapriye sukhamapi' iti smR^itisiddhatvena prAbalyamevakAroNAha | ayamarthaH naite sukhitveneshvareShyAH, tadapriyatvAt.h | yo yasyApriyaH sa sukhitvena na tadiShyaH, yathA rAjavirodhI rAj~na iti | nacha vyAptivachanavirodhaH, tasya tamovyatirikttaviShayatvena sAvakAshatvAditi | evaM cheshvarechChArUpakAraNAbhAvAnnAndhantamaH prAptAnAM sukhamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "loke' ityanena IshApriyatvAkhyaH sUchitaH |) || 15 || OM tatsvAbhAvyApattirupapatteH OM || ityatra, shabdAsya shaktayAdyanekavR^ittisadbhAvAt.h, "dhUmo bhUtvA' ityatra bhavanashabdArthaH kiM dhUmAdidaivataikyaM, uta tatpadaprAptiH, atha tatsvAbhAvyApattiriti sandehe, tadaikyaM, tatpadaprAptirveti pUrvaH pakShaH, tatsvAbhAvyApattiriti siddhAntaH | atrApi sahasthAnamityukttameva nyAyaM dvitIyapUrvapakShasAdhakatvena tAvadvivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha dhUmAdidevatAsahAvastAnAtkarmiNo.api tatpadaprAptiH | 
|| nacha dhUmAdIti || ayaM bhAvaH "dhUmo bhUtvA' iti sAmAnAdhikaraNyashrutirukttobhayarItyA yujyate, anyathA tadvirodhaH | nacha shruteranyathAtvaM kalpanIyam.h, bAdhakamantareNa mukhyArthatyAgAyogAt.h | nacha kamirNo daivataikyavat.h devatApadaprAptirapyasambhAvitA, dhUmAdidevatAbhiH sahAvasthAnAt.h snehAdivashena tAbhireva svapadAderdAnasyApi yukttatvAt.h | evaMcha karmiNo dhUmAdidevatAbhiH sahAvasthAnAdAkalpasamApti paramamukhyasAdhanatatpadaprAptisambhavAnna kamarNi vairAgyamApAdyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tatsvAbhAvyApattiH' ityanenaiva sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena pUrvokttameva "kAraNAbhAvaH' iti nyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
tannimittavidyAkhyakAraNAbhavAt.h || 16 || nacha taistaiH sahAvasthAnAdatichiratvam.h | 
|| tannimitteti || vidyetyupalakShaNam.h | "adhikAraH' ityapi grAhyam.h | karmiprApyatve, yugapadanekakarmisamavAye.anekeShAM yugapadanekapadaprAptiprasaN^gaH | nacha shruternairarthyam.h, tatsvabhAvaprAptereva bhavanashabdArthatvAt.h | nachAsyApi padaprAptiparyAyatvam.h, "tadgatau gatiH' ityAdyekadeshasvAbhAvatvAt.h | nacha shabdArthatyAgaH sAdR^ishye cha sAmAnAdhikaraNyaprayoMgadarshanAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha vidyAdikAraNAbhAvAt.h na karmiNAM dhUmAdidevatApadaprAptiriti ApAdyameva vairAgyAditi bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "upapatteH' ityanena vidyAkhyakAraNAbhAvena tatpadaprApteriti sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 16 || OM nAtichireNa visheShAt.h OM || ityatra, chirAchiragamanavishiShya(dvividha)pAnthadarshanena, karmiNaH svargAnnirgatya kiM chireNa garbhavAsaM prApnuvanti, utAchireNeti sandehe, chireNaiveti pUrvaH pakShaH, achireNeti siddhAntaH | atrApi sahasthAnamityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-  nacha taistairiti || dhUmAdidevairityarthaH | "AkAshAdvAyum.h' iti shrutau bahUnAmukttatvAt.h, "tairetaiH' iti vIpsA | tatashchAtichiratvamAgamanasyopapAditaM bhavati | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | tatratatra tatsvAbhAvyenAtimahAsukhe sambhavati, tadvihAyAgamane prayojanAbhAvAdityapi draShyavyam.h | evaMcha dhUmAdidevaiH sahAvasthAnAt.h, karmiNastallokAdAgamanasyAtichiratvena, tatraiva mahAsukhatvasambhavAt.h, na tatra vairAgyamApAdyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "nAtichireNa' ityanena, niShedhyatayA pUrvapakShasAdhyanirdeshashAttaddhetureva sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena pUrvokttameva "kAraNAbhAvaH' iti siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
vatsarAtpUrvameva tviti klR^iptakAlAdadhikAvasthAne kAraNAbhAvAt.h || 17 || nacha vrIhyAdijIvaiH sahAnavasthAnAdduHkhapraptiH | shabdavihitatvena pApAkhyakAraNAbhAvAt.h || 18 || 
|| vatsarAditi || nacha mahAsukhaprApteriShyatvena kAraNamiti vAchyam.h | na kamirNAM mahAsukhaprAptiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH visheShAdityanena vatsarAtpUrvameva tu iti pramANavisheShaklR^iptakAlAdadhikakAlAvasthAne kAraNAbhAva iti sUchitaH |) || 17 || OM anyAdhiShThite pUrvavadabhilapAt.h OM || ityatra, loke grAmAntaragamanasya duHkhahetutvadarshanAt.h, asya svargamArgasya puruShArthatvena kamirNaH svargAdAgamane duHkhavanto na veti sandehe, duHkhavanta iti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | atrApi sahasthAnamityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha vrIhyAdIti || na cheshvare vyabhichAraH, asvAtantyasya hetuvisheShaNatvAt.h | nachAsiddhiH, "ta iha vrIhiyavAH' iti teShAM vrIhyAdibhAvadarshanAt.h | na chAprayojakatA, vrIhyAdisahAvasthAne cha tachChedanAdinA duHkhaniyamAt.h | nahi duHkhinA sahAvasthAne.api duHkhaprAptAvIshvaravatsvAtantyaM pramitamastIti bhAvaH | tachcha duHkhaM yaj~nAdiphalameva, AgamanAderyaj~nAdiphalatvasya pratipAditatvAt.h | nacha duHkhakAraNAbhAvaH, yaj~nAnAM hiMsAyukttatvena tataH pApasya sambhavAditi pUrvapakShasheSho draShyavyaH | evaMcha sukhasAdhanatayA vedokttasya karmaNo yathA duHkhasAdhanatvaM, tathA vairAgyasyApIti na vairAgyamApAdyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "anyAdhiShThitaH' ityanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena prAgukttameva "kAraNAbhAvaH' iti siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- shabdavihitatveneti || "yaj~nAdeH' iti sheShaH | yaj~nAderhiMsAyutatve.api na pApahetutvam.h, niShiddhahiMsAyA eva tathAtvAt.h | yamAhiMsAyAH "agnIShomIyaM pashumAlabheta' iti

|| nacha pituriti || anyato.annAdeH | ayaM bhAvaH | mAtR^iyonipravesha eva tAvanna vidyate, "dehaM garbhasthitam.h' iti vachanAt.h | mAtR^ipraveshasadbhAve.api pitR^idvAraiveti na niyamaH, anyato.annAderapi praveshopapatteH | nanu sharIrapariNAmArthaM retaso.apekShitatvena pitR^ipraveshasyAvashyakatvaM pUrvAdhikaraNe samarthitamiti chenna, anyathA mAtR^istharetasaiva pariNAmopapatteH | prAgasiddhasharIraprAptira(pya)nupapannA, "dehaM garbhasthitaM kvApi' iti vachanena, mAturudarasthitagarbhasthitervA bahirnirgate vA pUrvasiddhadehapraveshasyokttatvAt.h | evaMcha sharIraprAptAvatiprayAsAbhAvAnnAtivairAgyamApAdyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo.anuvyAkhyAnokttarItyA pUrvasUtrAdanuvR^ittenAthashabdena prakArAntareNa jananasyoktteH sUchitaH |) taddhetutvenAnyAgatirityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- yonidvAreNeti || anyenAnyenaprakAreNAgatirgatyabhAvaH | gatyantarAbhAva iti yAvat.h | gatishabdena dehaprAptiruchyate | tatashcha sAmAnyata utsargataH anyenAnnadvArAdilakShaNaprakArAntareNAgatirdehaprAptyabhAva iti vivR^itaM bhavati | yadvA annAdidvAreNa mAtR^isharIraprAptyAdilakShaNavisheShajanane varAdirUpAnyA gatirasti sAmAnyato janane tu tAdR^ishagatyantarAbhAvAditi nyAyavivaraNAbhiprAyaH | nanu gatyantarAbhAvAt.h kathametadityata Aha-

|| pashchAdadR^iShyeriti ||  upalakShaNametat.h | pUrvamapItyapi grAhyam.h  | svapno nAmArthaj~nAtmakaH | tatra tAvat.h svApnAnAM karituragAdInAM parameshvarAyattatA nopapadyate, asatyatvAt.h | na tAvadime.anAdinityAH, svapnAvasthAntaH prAgUrdhvaM chopalabdhiprasaN^gAt.h | nahi vidyamAnA apyupalabdhisAdhaneShu chakShurAdiShvanuparateShu, nopalabhyante, upalabhyante choparateShviti sambhavati | nachAnyatragatAH, anyairapyanupalambhAt.h, | svApnAH padArthA nAnAdinityAH, madhyamaparimANopetatayA dR^ishyamAnatvAt.h ghaTavadityanumAnavirodhAchcha | nApyutpattivinAshavantaH, tathAtve.api, ghaTAdivatprAgUrdhvamupalambhaprasaktteH | nacha vAchyaM vidyudAdivattadaivotpattirvinAshashchAtaH prAgUrdhvamanupalambho na doShAyeti, itthambhAve pramANAbhAvAt.h, prAN^mR^idAdInAmUrdhvaM kapAlAdInAmanupalambhApatteshcha | nachaivaiShAM tatkAlIne janmani upAdAnaM nimittaM cha pashyAmaH | kartA cha na tAvajjIvAtmA, draShyurnirvyApAratvAt.h | aparasya chAdarshanAt.h | tathAcha yAvadvisheShabAdhe sAmAnyabAdhAnna sattvaM teShAm.h, avidyamAnAnekaturagakaryAdIn.h pashyAmItyuttarakAlInAnubhavavirodhAchcha | "svapnamAyAsarUpA' "svapnamanoratho yathA' ityAdishrutismR^itivirodhAchcheti | tadevaM na svApnAnAmarthAnAmIshvarAdhInatvam.h, nApi j~nAnasya, tasyApi nimittAbhAvenAparamArthatvAt.h | indriyapravR^ittInAmuparatatvAt.h | manaso bAhyArtheShvasvAtantAditi | evaMcha svapnasyAsatvAdasatashcheshvarAdhInatvAyogAnna tasya mahAmahimatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "sandhye sR^iShyiH' ityanena sUchitaH | tena pashchAdadR^iShyergatyuktteH pashchAdadR^iShyiH pUrvapakShanyAya ityukttaM bhavati |) taddhetutvenAshakyakartR^itAshakttiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti-

||j~nAnAj~nAnayorityAdinA || tachChabdena jIvaH parAmR^ishyate | aj~nAnAj~nAnAbhyAmeva svapnatirodhAnasambhavAtkimIshvareNeti vadatA pUrvapakShiNA j~nAnAj~nAnayarorIshvarabhinnatvamaN^gIkR^itameveti tannokttam.h | tathA cheshvaralakShmIbhinnatve sati, jIvabhinnatvaM jaDatve heturiti neshvarAdau vyabhichAraH shaN^kanIyaH | yadA chetanasya jIvasyAsvAtantyam.h, tadA kiM vAchyaM jaDarUpaj~nAnAj~nAnayorityabhipretya, kaimutyenetyukttam.h | tenaivAsvAtantyatayokttajIvenaiva | j~nAnAj~nAnayorapi jIvavadasvAtantAtprabodhahetutvAnupapattiriti bhAvaH | doShadvayApAtAditi || bhinnatvamAdAya jaDatvAtkaimutyenAsvAtantyaM, abhinnatvamAdAya jIvagatAsvAtantyamiti doShadvayApAtAdityarthaH | vyAhateriti || bhinnaM na bhavatItyuktte, abhinnamityevokttaM syAt.h, bhinnAbhinne.abhinnatvarAhityAbhAvAt.h, punarna bhavatItyuktte, vyAhatiH | evamabhinnaM na bhavatItyuktte, bhinnamityevokttaM syAt.h bhinnAbhinne bhedarAhityAbhAvAt.h, punarbhinnaM na bhavatItyuktte, vyAhatirityarthaH | aj~nAnAdeH svapnAdinimittatvasya pramANasiddhatavAdukttAnupapattiH kathaM chitparihartavyetyata Aha-
tAvanmAtranimittatve mAnAbhAvAt.h | sarvasyeshavashatve mAnAchcha || 2 || nacha kAlApekShayaiva jAgaritam.h achetanatvAdeva kAlasya | 
|| tAvanmAtreti || anubhavasya vidyamAnatvAtkathaM mAnAbhAva ityata ukttam.h- mAtreti || anubhavasya, j~nAnAj~nAnayornimittatvamAtraviShayatvamiti bhAvaH | na kevalaM svapnAderaj~nAnAdimAtranimittatve mAnAbhAvAdemaN^gIkAraH kiM tu Ishahetutve mAnasadbhAvAchchetyAha- sarvasyeti || anena jIvAderasvAtantyamapi pramApitaM bhavati | ata eva "svapnAdeH' ityanuktavA, sarvasyetyukttam.h | evaMcha jIvasya svataH svAtanteNa prabodhAbhAvAt.h, j~nAnAdInAM jaDatvena sutarAM svAtantAbhAvAdIshvarasyaiva svapnatirodhAnahetutvamiti bhAvaH | (atra pUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyau "tato hyasya bandhaviparyayau' ityanena dR^iShyAntAsvAtantyaj~nAnAj~nAnAdhInabandhamokShayoH paramAtmAdhInatvoktayA, "avij~nAnam.h', "svato bodhaH' iti kramAtsUchitau |) || 2 ||  OM dehayogAdvAso.api OM || ityatra, pUvarokttarItyA, jAgradavasthA kimIshvarAdhInA, na veti sandehe neti pUrvaH pakShaH, IshvarAdhIneti siddhAntaH | tatra "kAlaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha kAleti || evaMcha kAlApekShayA jAgaraNasya jAyamAnatvAnneshvarasya mahAmahimatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo - "vAso.api' ityapipadAt.h  "parAbhidhyAnAttu' ityasyAnukarShAdavadhAraNArthakatushabdena kAlaniShedhAtkAlAdhInatvaM jAgradavasthAyA iti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "tadeva' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- achetanatvAdeveti || etadanantaraM "asvAtantAt.h' iti grAhyam.h | tathAcha "tadeva' ityanuvyAkhyAne, tachChabdena "svato.abodhaH' ityatrAbhipretAsvAtantyasya nimittIbhUtAchetanatvasya parAmarsha iti bhAvaH | kAlasyAsvAtante kaimutyadyotanArthaM achetanatvAdevetyevakAraH tadevopapAdayati- chetanAntarasyeti || IshvaravyAvR^ittyarthamantaragrahaNam.h | kAlasya nimittamAtratvamiti bhAvaH | ata eva pUrvapakShe "kAlApekShayaiva' ityukttam.h | nanu mAstu kAlasyAchetanatvena, jAgaraNasya tadadhInatvam.h, tathApi neshvarAdhInatvaM sambhavati, jIvasya tadadhInatvAt.h | jAgaraNe hi jIvasya svAtantyaM pratIyata ityato vAha- 
chetanAntarasyApyasvAtantAt.h || 3 || nacha paramAtmano.anyatrAvasthAne duHkhitvaprApternADIShu suptirna bhavati | 
|| chetanAntarasyApIti || na kevalaM kAlasyetyapishabdaH | evaMcha kAlasyAchetanatvAdIshvarasyaiva jAgradavasthAprerakatvamiti, yukttaM tasya mahAmahimatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyA niShedhahetvAkAN^kShAyAmasvAtantyasyaiva taddhetutvasambhavAttatprayojakamachetanatvamityavadhAraNArthaka tushabdena sUchitaH |) || 3 || OM tadabhAvo nADIShu tachChruterAtmani OM || ityatra, "satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati' , "yatraitatsuptaH samastaH samprasannaH svapnaM na vijAnAtyAsu nADIShu supto bhavati' iti shrutibhyAM suptiH kiM bhagavati, nADIShu veti sandehe, bhagavatyeva, na nADIShviti pUrvaH pakShaH, nADIsthaparamAtmanIti 
siddhAntaH | tatra "duHkham.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha paramAtmana iti || duHkhitvaprApteriti jAgratsvapnayoH paramAtmano.anyatrAvasthAne duHkhitvadarshanAdityarthaH | nyAyasya pUrvapakShaphalasambandhastu mUla eva spaShyaH | vipakShabAdhakaitannyAyotprekShAmUlaM cha sUtre "nADIShu' iti padam.h | tena hi nADIsthaparamAtmani suptiriti, siddhAntapradarshanena, nADIShu suptirneti pUrvapakShanyAyaM pUrvapakShasAdhyaM dyotyate | tatra duHkhAbhAvo hetuH | tasyAprayojakatAparihArAyAnyathA "duHkhaM syAt.h' iti vipakShabAdhakatarkonnayanAt.h | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "Atmani' ityanena nADIShu suptyaN^gIkAre, duHkhaprAptiparihArakeNa sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "amAnaklR^iptiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
ubhayasvIkAropapattau mAnasya klR^iptyakAraNamityanavasthitidoShAdatiprasaN^gAt.h || 4 || nacha prabodhasya pR^ithagapi kAraNadR^iShyeH kvachittadeva | 
|| ubhayeti || nADIsthaparamAtmani suptyaN^gIkAreNa, nADIShu, paramAtmani chetyubhayasvIkAreNa pramANabhUtasya "satA somya tadA sampannaH' ,"nADIShu supto bhavati' iti shrutidvayasya vyavasthopapattau |) || 4 || OM ataH prabodho.asmAt.h OM || ityatra, sarvasya bhagavadadhInatvoktayA, suptiprabodho bhagavadhIna iti visheShAnuktayA cha, suptiprabodho bhagavadadhIno na veti sandehe, neshvaraikAdhIna ||desheti || khaNDeshaH kadAchideva kasyAJNchidavasthAyAmeva kAMshchinniyamayatItyarthaH | sachChabdArthaH- shrutIti || tatashchAnumAnaM bAdhitaviShayamiti bhAvaH | evaMcha sanmAnAdIshvarasyaiva sarvAvasthAprerakatvamiti yukttaM tasya mAhAtmyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH shabdapadena shrutimAnAdviShNoH sarvAvasthAprerakatvamiti sUchitaH |) || 6 || OM mugdhe.ardhasampattiH parisheShAt.h OM || ityatra, dvividhAvasthAdarshanAt.h, mohAvasthA kimIshvare, tadanyatra veti sandehe, Ishvara eveti pUrvaH pakShaH, Ishvare.ardhapriAptariti

| tathAcha mohaH prasiddhAvasthAbhyaH pR^ithak.h, anupapannAntarbhAve satyavasthAtvAditi parisheShAnumAnena, mohAvasthA pR^ithageva | mohasya pArthakye, kIdR^isho.asAviti chet.h, ardhaprAptiriti brUmaH | nacha tatra pramANAbhAvaH, parisheShasyaiva pramANatvAt.h | na tAvanmohe samagraprAptiH sambhavati, duHkhAnusandhAnAt.h | nApyaprAptiH anyArthAdarshanAt.h | "parisheShAt.h' ityanenokttaH |) || 7 || OM na sthAnato.api parasyobhayaliN^gaM sarvatra hi OM || ityatrAnekasthAnasthitAnAM ghaTAdInAM bhinnatvasyAkAshAdInAmabhinnatvasya darshanAtpratisharIraM || nacha sthAnabhedAditi || sthAnAnAM surAsuranarAdisharIrANAM, atrApi dakShiNAkShyAdInAM, bhedAdityarthaH | anena, sUtre sthAnashabdastadbhedopalakShaka ityukttaM bhavati | apipadena | AkAshasyaikadeshato.anekasthAnatvena, samagrarUpeNAnekasthAnatvAbhAvAt.h | nacha svarUpAsiddhiH, "saptAN^ga ekonaviMshatimukhaH' ityAdishrutisiddhatvAt.h | nacha "etameva brahmetyAchakShate' iti sthAnabhedAdIshvarasyApi bhinnatvAdbhinnAnAM cha guNatAratamyasyAnugrAhyAnugrAhakabhAvasya darshanAnna tasya mahAmahimatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "sthAnato.api' ityanena bhedaH, paramAtmano.abhedaH, iti vyavasthopapatteriti sUchitaH |) || 8 || OM arUpavadeva hi tatpradhAnatvAt.h OM || ityatra, yukttAyukttayoH sAdhanatvokttidarshanAdviShNuprAptisAdhanatvokttiryukttA, na veti sandehe, na yuktteti pUrvaH pakShaH, yukttaiveti siddhAntaH 
| tatra "viruddhatvam.h' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradasharnapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha rUpavattvArUpavattvavachanayorvirodhAdaprAmANyam.h | aprAkR^itarUpavattvamiti vyavasthopapatteH || 9 || 
|| nacha rUpavattveti || viShNuH kiM rUpavAn.h syAdutArUpavAn.h vA | nAdyaH | "tadarUpamanAmayam.h' ityAdyarUpatvAbhidhAyakashruteraprAmANyaprasaN^gAt.h | anityatvaprApteshcha | na dvitIyaH | "rugmavarNaM   kartAram.h'ityAdirUpapratipAdakashrutyaprAmANyApatteH | saundaryAdyabhAvaprasaN^gAchchetyarthaH | evaMcha shrutyoH parasparaM virodhAt.h, rUpAdyasiddhau, saundaryAdyayogena na paramAtmani bhakttiryuktteti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "prakAshavachchAvaiyarthyam.h' ityanena shrutivyavasthApradarshanena, rUpavattvArUpavattvavachanayorviruddhatvamiti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutve "vyavasthA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- aprakR^iteti || viShNoriti sheShaH | naJNo.abhAvArthatvena, prAkR^itarUpatvAbhAva ityapi vyAkhyeyam.h | tathAcha "rugmavarNam.h' ityAdishruteraprAkR^itarUpavattvapratipAdakatvaM "tadarUpam.h' ityAdishruteH prAkR^itarUpAbhAvapratipAdakatvamityanena prakAreNa vyavasthopapattevirrodhAbhAvena na vachanayAraprAmANyam.h | nApi saundaryAdyabhAvo.anityatvaprAptishcha, aprAkR^itarUpavattvAN^gIkArAt.h | anityatvaprAkR^itarUpAnaN^gIkArAdityarthaH | evaMcha vyavasthayA shrutiprAmANyAtsaundaryAdisambhavena, yukttA paramAtmani bhakttiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "prakAshavachchAvaiyarthyam.h' ityanena vilakShaNAprAkR^itarUpavattvena prAkR^itarUparAhityamiti sUchitaH |) || 9 || OM ata eva chopamAsUryakAdivat.h OM || ityatra, yukttAyukttasAdhanadarshanena, harau bhakttiryukttA, naveti sandehe, na yuktteti pUrvaH pakShaH, yuktteti siddhAntaH | tatra "nyAyasAmyam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha paramAtmano.achetanatvanyAyasAmyena jIvasyApi abhedaH alpaguNatvAdivirodhAt.h || 10 ||
|| nacha paramAtmaneti || paramAtmanAbheda ityanvayaH | chetanatve.apyupalakShaNam.h | apishabdo dR^iShyAntIbhUtamatsyAdisamuchchayArthaH | yadvA.abhedo.apIti sambandhaH | tena "bhedavyapadeshAchcha' ityAdinA jIvaparamAtmabhedasya pratipAditatvAt.h, kathaM tadabhedena pUrvapakShotthApanamityAshaN^kA parihR^itA bhavati | etadadhikaraNapUrvapakShiNA jIvabrahmaNoraMshAMshibhAvena, bhedAbhedAN^gIkArAdbhedAvirodhAt.h | evaMcha jIvaH, paramAtmAbhinnaH, chetanatvAt.h, aMshavat.h, matsyAdivat.h ityanumAnena jIvasya paramAtmAbhinnatvAtsvasmiMshcha vyaktayayogAnna bhakttiryuktteti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH bhedanirAsakachashabdena prAptasya nirAsAyogAditi tatprApakatvena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "alpatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- alpaguNatvAditi || "jIvasya' ityanuvartate | Adipadena paramAtmapratibimbatvaM gR^ihyate | yadvA paramAtmanaH pUrNaguNatvamAdishabdArthaH | tathAcha jIvaH paramAtmAbhinno na bhavati, tadviruddhadharmAdhikaraNatvAt.h, pratibimbatvAt.h, sampratipannavaditi anumAnavirodhAnna jIvasya paramAtmAbhedaH | nacha pUrvottarakAlAvasthAyibhinnAbhinne dehAdau vyabhichAraH, deshakAlapuruShAvasthAdibhedAnirbAdhaviruddhadharmAdhikaraNatvasya hetvarthAt.h | nacha chetanAMshatvanyAyavirodhaH, shrutyAdisiddhaitadanumAnena tayoreva bAdhitatvAt.h | evaMchAlpaguNatvAjjIvasya, anantaguNena paramAtmanAbhedAbhAvAdyukttA tatra bhakttiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH tadadhInatvAdyatharkeNa "ata eva' ityanena sUchitaH | tadapekShayAlpatAM vinA tadadhInatvAyogAt.h |) || 10 || OM ambuvadagrahaNAttu na tathAtvaM OM || ityatra, kartavyAkartavyArthadarshanAdbhagavadbhakttiH kartavyA, na veti sandehe, na kartavyeti pUrvaH pakShaH, kartavyeti siddhAntaH | tatra "satobhava' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradasharnapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha sAdR^ishyasya satvAtsAdhanaM vinaiva jIvasya tAdR^iktavavyakttiH anAditaH saMsArasyAnivR^ittatvena bhAvAt.h || 11 || 
|| nacha sAdR^ishyasyeti || satvAnnityamiti sheShaH | sAdhanaM vinaivaiti || vidyamAnasya kadAchitsvayameva suptAvivAbhivyakttisambhavAditi bhAvaH | tAdR^iktavaM j~nAnAnandAdisAdR^ishyam.h, anena, "sato bhavaH' sattvamiti nyAyo vivR^ito bhavati | evaMcha j~nAnAnandAdisAdR^ishyasyAnAditaH satvena, bhakttiM vinaivAbhivyakttisambhavAnna tadarthaM mAhAtmyavarNanamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tathAtvam.h' ityanena vidyamAnasyAbhivyakttatvamiti vadatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "bhavaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- anAdita iti || nachAprayojako hetuH | j~nAnAnandAdisAdR^ishyasya sAdhanaM vinaivAbhivyakttatvenAnAdisaMsArapravAhAnupapatte | evaMchAnAditaH saMsArasya sadbhAvAt.h, j~nAnAnandAdisAdR^ishyAbhivyaktayarthaM harau bhakttiH kartavyeti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "na tathAtvam.h' ityanena sato.apyanabhivyakttatvaM vadatA sUchitaH |) || 11 || OM vR^iddhihrAsabhAktavamantarbhAvAdubhayasAmaJNjasyAdevam.h OM || ityatra, ekaprakAreNa chetanatvAdInAM tAratamyopetaj~nAnAdInAM dharmANAM darshanena, bhagavadbhakttiH kiM bhaktteShvekaprakArA, uta vR^iddhihrAsavatIti sandehe, ekaprakAraiveti pUrvaH pakShaH, vR^iddhihrAsavatIti 
siddhAntaH | tatra guNasAmyamityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha mukttatvAdiguNasAmyAdbrahmAdInAM bhaktayAdiguNasAmyam.h | yathAyathAdhikAro vishiShyate evaM j~nAnaM bhakttirbalaM cha vishiShyate |
|| nacha mukttatvAditi || tatra mukttatvaM nAma saMsAranivR^ittiH | tasyAH sarvatra sAmyam.h  | AdishabdenAnandatvAdi grAhyam.h | atra, guNasAmyamityetat.h sAdhyahetupratipAdakatvena dvedhA vivR^itamiti j~nAtavyam.h | nachAprayojako hetuH, kAlasAmyeti, sAdhanAtishayena svavaiyarthyaM keShAJNchidasamyagbhakttirvA syAditi | evaMcha phalabhUtamukttatvAdisAmyAt.h, sAdhanabhUtabhaktayAderapi na tAratamyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "adarshanAchcha' iti sUtreNa mukttatvAdiphalatAratamyaM pratipAdayatA sUchitaH | anyathA tatkathanamasaN^gataM syAt.h |) taddhetutvena "viAsheShadR^iShyiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- yathAyatheti || adhikAraH shravaNAdau | ete j~nAnabhaktayAdayaH mukttAveteShAM phalatvenAN^gIkArAt.h | brahmaNe chaturmukhAya, visheShadR^iShyeH sAdhyasAdhanatAratamyadarshanAdityarthaH | evaMcha sAdhyasAdhanatAratamyadarshanAdityarthaH | evaMcha sAdhyasAdhanatAratamyalakShaNavisheShasya shrutyA dR^iShyerna bhaktayAdisAdhanasyaikaprakArateti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "adarshanAchcha' ityanenaiva sUtreNa visheShadR^iShyirvisheShashrutirityukttaH |) || 12 || OM prakR^itaitAvattvaM hi pratiShedhati tato bravIti cha bhUyaH OM || ityatra guNAnAmapi cha yukttAyukttatvadarshanAjjagatpAlakatvarUpo guNo viShNoryuktto na veti sandehe, na yuktta iti pUrvaH pakShaH, yuktta iti siddhAntaH | tatra "ayogaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
mukttAvAnanda ete cha guNA vishiShyanta ata AhurbrahmaNe mukttA baliM harantItyAdivisheShadR^iShyeH || 12 || nacha saMhArakarturasaMhArAdanyarakShAyA ayogaH sa sR^ijati sa pAlayati sa vinAshayati ityAdivisheShavAkyAt.h | 
|| nacha saMhAreti || anyasya saMhAre sati, tannivAraNAdirUpo vyApAro.asaMhAraH, saMhArAnyo rakShArUpaH sambhavet.h, na chaivamiti bhAvaH | evaMcha asaMhAravyatirikttarakShAyA ayogena pAlakatvAbhAvAnna tasya mahAmahimatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH tato bravIti cha bhUyaH ityanena, pAlakatvasya sR^iShyisaMhArakartR^itvAdbhinnatvaM pratipAdayatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShavAkyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM tadvAkyodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- sa sR^ijamiti || sa pAlayatIti pR^ithaguktterasya visheShavAkyatvaM j~nAtavyam.h  | anena "visheShadR^iShyivAkye' ityanuvyAkhyAne visheShapadasyobhayatrApyanvaya ityukttaM bhavati | vAkye cheti chashabdasamuchchitanyAyamAha- 
annadAnAdyupapatteshcha || 13 || na chAvyakttasvabhAvasya darshane tarkabAdhaH | anantashakttitvAdviShNoH tachChaktayAvyakttasyApi darshanopapatteH || 14 || 
|| annadAneti ||  annadAnAdirUpopapatterityarthaH | asaMhAravyatirikttapAlanAbhAve.annadAnAdi na syAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha visheShavAkyAt.h pAlanAdiyuktterharau bhakttiryuktteti bhAvaH | ayaM cha nyAyo "bravIti cha' ityanenokttaH |) || 13 || OM tadavyakttamAha hi OM || ityatra, katarvyAkartavyavyApAradarshanAdbhakttiH kartavyA na veti sandehe, na kartavyeti pUrvaH pakShaH, kartavyeti siddhAntaH | tatra "tarkabAdhaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM apekShitAMshapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- nachAvyaktteti || avyakttasvabhAvasya Ishvarasya, darshane, Ishvaro na pratIyate, avyakttasvabhAvatvAt.h, adR^iShyavaditi tarkabAdha ityarthaH | atra, neshvare bhakttiH kAryA prayojanAbhAvAt.h | nacha tadAparokShyaM prayojanamiti vAchyam.h | tasyAvyakttasvabhAvatvenAparokShyatarkabAdha iti pUrvapakShyabhiprAyaH | evaMcha tarkabAdhena bhagavadApArokShyAbhAvena, bhaktterniShphalatvAnna yukttaM mAhAtmyavarNanamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "tadavyakttamAha hi' ityAdisUtratrayeNa jIvashaktayA j~nAnAbhAve.avyakttatvarUpahetuM vadatA sUchitaH | tathA "prakAshashcha karmaNyabhyAsAt.h' ityanena chakAreNIAvyakttatvasamuchchayAdavyakttatve.api prakAsho bhavatItyavyakttatvasyAprayojakatvoktayA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "puMshakttiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- anantashakttitvAditi || avyakttasvabhAvasya svaprasAdenApi pratyakShatA na yujyate | nahi prasanno.api naro vAnaro bhavitumIShya ityAshaN^kAparihArAtharmetadukttam.h | tachChaktayA viShNushaktayA, anena "puMshakttiH' ityatra puMshabdo viShNuvAchaka ityukttaM bhavati | evaM chAvyakttasyApi puMshaktayAparokShyasambhavAdyukttA tatra bhakttiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "ato.anantena tathA hi liN^gam.h' ityanenAnantashakttitvAdviShNostachChaktayA prakAshopapatterityarthaH |) || 14 || OM ubhayavyapadeshAttvahikuNDalavat.h OM || ityatra, pUrvAdhikaraNavat.h sabIjaH sandehaH, pUrvaH pakShaH, siddhAntashcha | tatra "vilomatA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha guNAnAM guNisvarUpatvaM viruddham.h  kAlAdidR^iShyAntAt.h || 15 || 
|| nacha guNAnAmiti || evaMcha guNAnAM guNitvasvarUpatvavilomatayeshvarasya guNitvAbhAvAnna yukttA tatra bhakttiriti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "ubhayavyapadeshAt.h' ityanenAnAditvamAnandatvaM cha sAdhayatA guNasya guNisvarUpatvaM viruddhamiti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "sunidarshanam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- kAlAdIti || yathA kAlasya pUrveNAbhede.api, "kAlaH' iti visheShyaH, "pUvarH' iti visheShako bhavati | yathA vA prakAshAtmakasyApyAdityasya prakAshitvam.h, yathA vA kuNDalAtmasyApyaheH kuNDalitvam.h, (evaM) visheShabalAdeva, guNAtmakasyApi brahmaNaH AnandavattvAdikaM yujyata iti bhAvaH | atrAhikuNDaladR^iShyAntasya sthUlamatInAM buddhayArohanimittatvena, dvitIyatR^itIyayostejorUpatvAtisUkShmatvAbhyAM brahmaNa AdityakAlasAmyAt.h, anurUpatvena bahurUpatvena cha, dR^iShyAntAnAM suShThutvamanuvyAkhyAyAM sushabdenokttam.h | tachchAnantarokttasyApi kAladR^iShyAntasya prathamaM grahaNena bahatvapradarshakeNAdipadena vivR^itam.h | ahikuNDaladR^iShyAntasya bhedAbhedaviShayatvena, kAlAdivadAnurUpyAbhAvAt.h | evaMcha kAlAdinidarshanena guNasvarUpasyApi harerguNitvena, yukttA tatra bhakttiriti bhAvaH | ayaM cha nyAyaH "ahikuNDalavat.h' "prakAshAshrayavadvA' "pUrvavadvA'  ityanenokttaH |) || 15 || OM paramataH setUnmAnasambandhabhedavyapadeshebhyaH OM || ityatra, bhagavadAnandAdiguNAnAM laukikatvAlaukikatvasya na sambhavAllaukikatvAlaukikatvasandehe, lokasadR^ishamevAnandAdikamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, alaukikamiti siddhAntaH | tatra "vilomatA' ityanena pUrvapakShokttanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha brahmAdInAmanyathAtvAttadatachChabdatvaM tachChabdatve lokopamatvaM cheti vilomatA alaukikAstasya shabdAstathArthA alaukiko hyeSha viShNuH paratvAt.h | tathApi shabdA laukikA apyamuShmin.h pravartamAnA adhikArthAn.h vadantItyAdi shrutibhyo.alaukikatvAvagamAt.h || 16 ||
|| nacha brahmeti || tatra anyathAtvAdityalaukikalakShaNApAdakameva huetutayokttam.h | atachChabdatvaM AnandAdishabdavAchyatvAbhAvaH syAdityarthaH | tachChabdatve, AnandAdishabdavAchyatve, lokopamatvaM syAditi sheShaH | evaM chAlaukikatve AnandAdishabdavAchyatvAbhAvaH, laukikeShveva saN^gatigrahaNAt.h | AnandAdishabdavAchyatve cha, laukikatvamiti, alaukikatvAnandAdivAchyatvayorvilomatayA, sahAnavasthAnalakShaNavirodhitayA, AnandAdishabdavAchyatvena laukikAnandAdiguNe paramAtmani bhakttirna yuktteti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "buddhayarthaH pAdavat.h' ityanena alaukikatvAnandAdishabdavAchyatvayorvirodhaM pariharatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "alaukikatvam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- alaukikA iti || shabdAnAmalaukikatvaM nAma vaidikatvam.h | arthAnAmalaukikatvaM nAmAprAkR^itatvam.h | arthAH nyAyaM vivR^iNoti- alaukikA iti || shabdAnAmalaukikatvaM nAma vaidikatvam.h | arthAnAmalaukikatvaM nAmAprAkR^itatvam.h | arthAH AnandAdiguNAH | kuta ityata ukttam.h- alaukiko hIti | tadapi kuta ityata ukttam.h- paratvAditi || uttamatvAdityarthaH | laukikAH pauruSheyAgamAH adhikArthAn.h lokavilakShaNAnandAdIn.h alaukikatvAvagamAt.h, "brahmAnandAdInAm.h' iti sheShaH | evaMchaitachChrutivirodhAdalaukikatvAnandAdishabdavAchyatvayorna virodha iti brahmAnandAdelalaukikatve.api, AnandAdishabdavAchyatvamupapannamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "paramataH' ityanena "darshanAt.h' ityanena chokttaH |) || 16 || OM sthAnavisheShAtprakAshAdivat.h OM || ityatra, padArthAnAM kiJNchitpratibimbatvApratibimbatvadarshanena, chaturmukhAdyAnandAdibhagavadAnandAdipratibimbaM bhavati na veti sandehe, pratibimbaM na bhavatIti pUrvaH pakShaH, bhagavadAnandAdipratibimbamiti siddhAnta ;| tatra "mAnAbhAvaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha brahmAdyAnandavaichitye bimbabhUtaviShNvAnandavaichityam.h AdityAdivadAdhikyAt.h | 
|| nacha brahmeti || atra brahmAdyAnandavaichityasyAprayojakatvaM vadatA pUrvapakShe pratibimbabhUtabrahmAdyAnandavaichitye, brahmabhUtaviShNvAnandavaichityaM syAt.h, anyathA brahmAdyAnandavaichityaM na syAditi tarkaH "nAnA bhAvaH' ityanenoktta iti vivR^itaM bhavati | evaMcha pratibimbabhUtabrahmAnandAdInAM nAnAbhAvAdvichitratvAdbimbabhUtaviShNvAnandAderapi vaichityApAtena, na tatra bhakttirupapanneti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "sthAnavisheShAt.h' ityanena, brahmAnandadInAM nAnAbhAvasyAnyathAsiddhiM pratipAdayatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "Adhikyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- AdityAdivaditi || Adipadena, sUryakAntAdisthAnaM gR^ihyate | AdhikyAditi bimbabhUtaviShNoraishvaryarUpAdhikyAdbrahmAdisthAnAnAM bhaktayAdiguNairAdhikyAdityarthaH | sthAnashaktayapekShayA bimbashakttermukhyatvAtsautrakramollaN^ghanam.h | sautrakramamanusR^ityAdipadokttadR^iShyAntamupapAdayati- 
nahi sUryakAntapratibimbasyAgnijanakatvashakttirna jalagatasyetyetAvatA sUrye vaichityam.h | AdhikyaM hi tatra nimittam.h | 
sUryachandrAdipratibimbaM vinAnyatra tathA visheShAdR^iShyeH || 17 || 
|| nahIti || madhyamapadalopena, sUryakAntAdigatAdityapratibimbasyetyatharH | tathAcha, yathA sUryakAntAdigatasUrya pratibimbasyAgnijanakatvaM na jalagatasyeti pratibimbavaichityeti, na bimbe sUrye vaichityam.h, tathA brahmadyAnandavaichitye.api na bhagavadAnandavaichityamiti bhAvaH | anena sUryakAntAdigatasUryapratibimbasUvaryakAntAdau mitho vichitratvahetorvyabhichAra uktto bhavati | nanu bimbavaichityAbhAvAtsUryakAntagatasUryapratibimbasyAgnijanakatvashakttirna jalagatasyetyatra kiM nimittamityata Aha- AdhikyaM hIti || "sUryAdigatamityarthaH | tadupapAdayati- sUryeti || sUryachandrAdeH pratibimbaM vinAnyatra sUryakAntAdigata mukhe.agnijanakatvarUpavisheShAdR^iShyerityarthaH | anena AdityetyukttadR^iShyAnta upapAdito bhavati | evaMcha bimbabhUtaviShNvaishvaryA dyAdhikyAtsthAnabhUtabrahmAdInAM bhaktayAdiguNAdhikyAdbrahmAdyAnandavaichitye.api na viShNvAnandavaichityamiti yukttA tatra bhakttiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "sthAnavisheShAt.h' iti brahmAdisthAnAdhikyaM vadatA "upapatteshcha' ityanena, bhagavata aishvaryarUpAdhikyaM vadatA chokttaH |) || 17 || OM tathAnyatpratiShedhAt.h OM || ityatra, vyakttAvyakttapadArthadarshanAdbrahma kimavyakttaM, vyakttamiti sandehe, vyakttamiti pUvarH pakShaH, avyakttamiti siddhAntaH | tatra "mAnAbhAvaH' ityukttapUvarpakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha nAnAbhAvAdviShNoshchittapratibimbarUpatA AdhikyAdeva | pratibimbe hi doShAshcha pratIyante | ato hi shrutiH pratiShedhati "nedaM yadidamupAsata iti || 18 || 
|| nacha nAnAbhAvAditi || rUpANAmiti sheShaH | viShNorityasya rUpANAmityAdhyAhR^itenApi sambandhaH | chittapratibimbarUpatA dhyAnakAle pratItachittopAdAnakatvetyarthaH | tatashchAyamarthaH | viShNoH svarUpabhedAbhAve.api dhyAtR^ibahutvena, dhyAnakAle pratItarUpANAM bahutvena, teShAM viShNutvAN^gIkAre virodhAbhAvAdviShNoshchittapratibimbarUpatetyavyakttatvAbhAvAdvayarthA bhakttiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "anyat.h' ityanena viShNuchittapratibimbayorbhedaM samarthayatA nAnAbhAvAdviShNoshchittapratibimbatatvaM sambhavatIti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "Adhikyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- AdhikyAdeveti || evashabdena sUtragatatathAshabdAbhiprAya uktto bhavati | yathA khalu jIvAnandAdInAM alpatvAdinA kAraNena brahmAnandAderunmAnatvAdAdhikyAttato vailakShaNyam.h tathA prakR^itasya chittaprakR^itibimbasya durlakShaNatvAdikAraNena viShNornidoॅShatvAdyAdhikyAdeva tadvailakShaNyamiti | viShNorAdhikye.api, kuto na chittapratibimbarUpatetyAha- pratibimbe hIti || atra shrutyavaShyambhamapyAha- ato hIti || hishabdaH shruteH prasiddhatAM dyotayati | nirdoShadoShitvavailakShaNyena brahmopAsAprakR^itayoraikyAnupapatterityarthaH | aikye shrautaniShedho na syAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha viShNornirdoShatvAdyAdhikyAchchittapratibimbarUpatvAbhAvAdyukttamavyakttatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tathA' ityanena, chittapratItasya durlakShaNayukttatvAdviShNornirdoShatvenAdhikyAditi sUchitaH | ata eva tatvaprakAshikAyAM dR^iShyAntadArShyAntikayoH sahetukayorvyAkhyAnaM kR^itam.h |) || 18 || OM anena sarvagatatvamAyAmayashabdAdibhyaH OM || ityatra, "janmAdyasya' yata ityAdijagatkartR^itvAdyuktteH yatkiJNchijjagatkartR^itve sakalajagatkartR^itve vA sambhavAtparameshvaraH kiM sarvadeshakAlInasR^iShyayAdikartA, na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, sarvadeshakAlInasR^iShyayAdikarteti siddhAntaH | tatra "nAnAbhAvaH' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatphalapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha nAnAvatArakautukadarshanAdviShNoH kvachiddeshakAlAntare kautukAdeva sR^iShyayAdi kurvan.h anyameva sAmastyena niyojayati sarvatra sarvametasmAdityAdishrutyA krIDAyAmapi svAtantAt.h | svAtantAtkrIDate viShNurna cha svAtantyamanyagam.h | karoti kvApi niyatA krIDA sR^iShyayAdikAsya cha || 
|| nacha nAnAvatAreti || anekAvatAre kautukasya kR^iShNAdyavatAreShu lIlArUpakautukasya, darshanAt.h kautukAdeva lIlayaiva, sAmastyena svAtantAdinA, taddatveti yAvat.h | niyojayati sR^iShyayAdAvityarthaH | evaMcha viShNoravatAreShu nAnAkautukadarshanAjjagatsR^iShyayAdikartR^itvamapyanyasmai dAsyatIti na tasyaiva mahAmahimatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH sAvadhAraNena "anena' ityanenAnyasya jagatsR^iShyayAdi nirAkurvatA IshvarAvatAreShu nAnAbhAvadarshanAdanyasmai jagatsR^iShyayAdikartR^itvadAnopapatteriti sUchitaH | ata eva bhAShye "anenaiva' iti |) taddhetutvena "svAtantyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- sarvatreti || Adipadena "sarvadA sarvavastuShu' iti vAkyasheSho grAhyaH | svAtantAt.h svAtantAvagamAdityarthaH | sarvatra sarvavastuShu, sarvavastuviShayaM sarvasR^iShyayAdyetasmAdbhavatIti sheShaH | tathA yadi krIDayAnyasmai dadyAttarhi ttakAlInasR^iShyayAdikartR^itvAbhAvaprAptyA, 
sarvavastuviShayasarvadeshakAlInasR^iShyayAdikartR^itvapratipAdakashrutivirAdhaH syAdityarthaH | atrArthe spaShyashrutiM chAha- svAtantAtkrIData iti || kvApi deshe kAle cha, niyatAsyeti sambandhaH sR^iShyayAdikAsR^iShyayAdiviShayA iti | niyataM sR^iShyayAdiviShayaM, evaMcha svAtantAttasyaiva sakaladeshakAlInajagatsR^iShyayAdikartR^itvAdyukttA tatra bhakttiriti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "sarvagataH' iti padenaiva sarvaishvaryAdirUpaH sUchitaH |) || 19 || OM phalamata upapatteH OM || ityatra, vAdivipratipattyA kiM hariH phaladAtA, kiM vA karma dAtriti sandehe, kamaraiva phaladAtriti pUrvaH pakShaH, IshvaraH phaladAteti siddhAntaH | tatra "pralobhaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM sahetukaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
niyatakrIDanAdeva kartA nAnyo.asti kasyachit.h | asvatantro hi chalati chalachittAdashakttitaH | svatantraH pUrNashakttiH sankuto.asau niyatiM tyajediti shruteshcha || 19 || nacha karmAnvayavyatirekAtphalasyeshvaraH | phaladAteti pralobhamAtram.h tasyaiva svAtantAt.h | karmANyanantAni yatheShyamIshaH sampAdya teShAM phalamichChayaiva |
|| nacha karmAnvayeti || anvayavyatirekAditi samAhAradvandvaH | evaMcheshvaraH phalapradAtetyatra pralobhanamAtratvAnna niratishayaishvaryamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "dharmaM jaiminirata eva' ityanena phaladAtuH karmaNo.api bhagavadadhInatvoktayA, karmAnvayavyatirekAtphalasya, Ishvarasya phaladAtR^itvaM pralobhanamAtramiti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "svAtantyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- tasyaiveti || Ishvarasyaiva karmAprayojyatvena phaladAtre kartR^itvAt.h ityatharH | svAtantAdityanena karmeshvarayoH sAmyaM niShedhati | tena karmaNaH phalanimittakAraNatvenAnvayavyatirekayoranyathAsiddhirukttA bhavati | atra pramANamAha- 
kvachiddadAti kva cha nodadAti nahyAnantyAtkarmaNAM bhoganAshaH | svAtantyaM chetkarmaNAM sarvabhogaH syAnnahyevaM kvApi tatkena chitsyAt.h |
